class AvlNode<K : Comparable<K>, V>(
    key: K,
    value: V,
    left: AvlNode<K, V>? = null,
    right: AvlNode<K, V>? = null,
    var height: Int = 1
) : Node<K, V, AvlNode<K, V>>(key, value, left, right)

class AvlTree<K : Comparable<K>, V> : Tree<K, V> {
    private var root: AvlNode<K, V>? = null
    var size = 0

    private fun height(node: AvlNode<K, V>?): Int {
        return node?.height ?: 0
    }

    private fun updateHeight(node: AvlNode<K, V>?) {
        node?.height = 1 + maxOf(height(node.left), height(node.right))
    }

    private fun balanceFactor(node: AvlNode<K, V>?): Int {
        return if (node == null) 0 else height(node.left) - height(node.right)
    }

    private fun minNode(node: AvlNode<K, V>): AvlNode<K, V> {
        var current: AvlNode<K, V> = node
        while (current.left != null) {
            current = current.left!!
        }
        return current
    }
}abstract class Node<K : Comparable<K>, V, N : Node<K, V, N>>(
    var key : K,
    var value : V,
    var left: N? = null,
    var right: N? = null
)

interface Tree<K : Comparable<K>, V> : Iterable<Pair<K, V>> {
    fun insert(key: K, value: V)
    fun delete(key: K)
    fun search(key: K): V?
}
enum class NodeColor {
    RED, BLACK
}

class RBNode<K : Comparable<K>, V>(
    key: K,
    value: V,
    left: RBNode<K, V>? = null,
    right: RBNode<K, V>? = null,
    var parent: RBNode<K, V>? = null,
    var color: NodeColor = NodeColor.RED,
) : Node<K, V, RBNode<K, V>>(key, value, left, right)

class RBTree<K : Comparable<K>, V> : Tree<K, V> {
    private var root: RBNode<K, V>? = null

    private fun rotateLeft(x: RBNode<K, V>?) {         //x        y
        val y = x?.right ?: return                     // \  ->  /
                                                       //  y    x
        x.right = y.left
        y.left?.parent = x

        val parent = x.parent
        y.parent = parent

        when {
            parent == null -> root = y
            x == parent.left -> parent.left = y
            else -> parent.right = y
        }

        y.left = x
        x.parent = y
    }

    private fun rotateRight(x: RBNode<K, V>?) {        // x     y
        val y = x?.left ?: return                     // /  ->   \
                                                     // y         x
        x.left = y.right
        y.right?.parent = x

        val parent = x.parent
        y.parent = parent

        when {
            parent == null -> root = y
            x == parent.right -> parent.right = y
            else -> parent.left = y
        }

        y.right = x
        x.parent = y
    }

    private fun fixAfterInsert(node: RBNode<K, V>) {
        var current: RBNode<K, V>? = node

        while (current != root && current?.parent?.color == NodeColor.RED) {
            val grandparent = current.parent?.parent

            if (current.parent == grandparent?.left) {
                val uncle = grandparent?.right

                if (uncle?.color == NodeColor.RED) {
                    current.parent?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    uncle.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    grandparent.color = NodeColor.RED
                    current = grandparent
                } else {
                    if (current == current.parent?.right) {
                        val parent = current.parent

                        if (parent != null) {
                            current = parent
                            rotateLeft(current)
                        }
                    }

                    current.parent?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    grandparent?.color = NodeColor.RED
                    rotateRight(grandparent)
                }
            } else {
                val uncle = grandparent?.left

                if (uncle?.color == NodeColor.RED) {
                    current.parent?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    uncle.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    grandparent.color = NodeColor.RED
                    current = grandparent
                } else {
                    if (current == current.parent?.left) {
                        current = current.parent
                        rotateRight(current)
                    }

                    current?.parent?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    grandparent?.color = NodeColor.RED
                    rotateLeft(grandparent)
                }
            }
        }

        root?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
    }
}package bst

import tree.BinNode
import tree.Tree

class BinTree<K: Comparable<K>, V>: Tree<K, V> {
    private var root: BinNode<K, V>? = null

    override fun insert(key: K, value: V) {
        if (root == null) {
            root = BinNode(key, value)
            return
        }

        var current = root

        while (current != null) {
            when {
                key < current.key -> {
                    if (current.left == null) {
                        current.left = BinNode(key, value)
                        return
                    }
                    current = current.left
                }

                key > current.key -> {
                    if (current.right == null) {
                        current.right = BinNode(key, value)
                        return
                    }
                    current = current.right
                }

                else -> {
                    current.value = value
                    return
                }
            }
        }
    }

    override fun delete(key: K) {
        root = deleteNode(root, key)
    }

    private fun deleteNode(binNode: BinNode<K, V>?, key: K): BinNode<K, V>? {
        binNode ?: return null

        when {
            key < binNode.key -> binNode.left = deleteNode(binNode.left, key)
            key > binNode.key -> binNode.right = deleteNode(binNode.right, key)
            else -> {
                if (binNode.left == null && binNode.right == null) {
                    return null
                }
                if (binNode.left == null) {
                    return binNode.right
                }
                if (binNode.right == null) {
                    return binNode.left
                }

                val minNode = findMin(binNode.right!!)
                binNode.key = minNode.key
                binNode.value = minNode.value
                binNode.right = deleteNode(binNode.right, minNode.key)
            }
        }
        return binNode
    }

    private fun findMin(binNode: BinNode<K, V>): BinNode<K, V> {
        var current = binNode
        while (current.left != null) {
            current = current.left!!
        }
        return current
    }

    override fun search(key: K): V? {
        var current = root

        while (current != null) {
            when {
                key < current.key -> current = current.left
                key > current.key -> current = current.right
                else -> return current.value
            }
        }

        return null
    }

    override fun iterator(): Iterator<Pair<K, V>> {
        val result = mutableListOf<Pair<K, V>>()
        val queue = ArrayDeque<BinNode<K, V>>()

        if (root != null) {
            queue.add(root!!)
        }

        while (queue.isNotEmpty()) {
            val current = queue.removeFirst()
            result.add(current.key to current.value)

            if (current.left != null) {
                queue.add(current.left!!)
            }
            if (current.right != null) {
                queue.add(current.right!!)
            }
        }

        return result.iterator()
    }
}package tree

open class BinNode<K: Comparable<K>, V>(
    var key: K,
    var value: V,
    var left: BinNode<K, V>? = null,
    var right: BinNode<K, V>? = null
)package tree

interface Tree<K: Comparable<K>, V>: Iterable<Pair<K, V>>{
    fun insert(key: K, value: V)
    fun delete(key: K)
    fun search(key: K): V?
}package bst

import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.assertEquals
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.assertNull
import kotlin.test.assertTrue
import kotlin.text.insert

class BinTreeTest {

    @Test
    fun searchInEmptyTreeReturnsNull() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        assertNull(tree.search(10))
    }

    @Test
    fun insertOneElementAndFindIt() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")

        assertEquals("five", tree.search(5))
    }

    @Test
    fun insertSeveralElementsAndFindThem() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")

        assertEquals("five", tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("three", tree.search(3))
        assertEquals("seven", tree.search(7))
    }

    @Test
    fun insertExistingKeyReplacesValue() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "old")
        tree.insert(5, "new")

        assertEquals("new", tree.search(5))
    }

    @Test
    fun searchMissingKeyReturnsNull() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")

        assertNull(tree.search(10))
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteFromEmptyTreeDoesNothing() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.delete(10)

        assertNull(tree.search(10))
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteLeaf() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")

        tree.delete(3)

        assertNull(tree.search(3))
        assertEquals("five", tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("seven", tree.search(7))
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteNodeWithOnlyLeftChild() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(2, "two")

        tree.delete(3)

        assertNull(tree.search(3))
        assertEquals("two", tree.search(2))
        assertEquals("five", tree.search(5))
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteNodeWithOnlyRightChild() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(8, "eight")

        tree.delete(7)

        assertNull(tree.search(7))
        assertEquals("eight", tree.search(8))
        assertEquals("five", tree.search(5))
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteNodeWithTwoChildren() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(6, "six")
        tree.insert(8, "eight")

        tree.delete(7)

        assertNull(tree.search(7))
        assertEquals("six", tree.search(6))
        assertEquals("eight", tree.search(8))
        assertEquals("five", tree.search(5))
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteRoot() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")

        tree.delete(5)

        assertNull(tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("three", tree.search(3))
        assertEquals("seven", tree.search(7))
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteRootWithOneChild() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")

        tree.delete(5)

        assertNull(tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("three", tree.search(3))
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteMissingKeyDoesNothing() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")

        tree.delete(10)

        assertEquals("five", tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("three", tree.search(3))
        assertEquals("seven", tree.search(7))
    }

    @Test
    fun iteratorOnEmptyTree() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        val result = tree.toList()

        assertTrue(result.isEmpty())
    }

    @Test
    fun iteratorReturnsElementsInBFSOrder() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(2, "two")
        tree.insert(4, "four")

        val result = tree.toList()

        assertEquals(
            listOf(
                5 to "five",
                3 to "three",
                7 to "seven",
                2 to "two",
                4 to "four",
            ), result)
    }

    @Test
    fun iteratorWorksCorrectlyAfterDeletion() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(6, "six")
        tree.insert(8, "eight")

        tree.delete(7)

        val result = tree.toList()

        assertEquals(
            listOf(
                5 to "five",
                3 to "three",
                8 to "eight",
                6 to "six"
            ), result)
    }
}class AvlNode<K : Comparable<K>, V>(
    key: K,
    value: V,
    left: AvlNode<K, V>? = null,
    right: AvlNode<K, V>? = null,
    var height: Int = 1
) : Node<K, V, AvlNode<K, V>>(key, value, left, right)

class AvlTree<K : Comparable<K>, V> : Tree<K, V> {
    private var root: AvlNode<K, V>? = null
    var size = 0

    private fun height(node: AvlNode<K, V>?): Int {
        return node?.height ?: 0
    }

    private fun updateHeight(node: AvlNode<K, V>?) {
        node?.height = 1 + maxOf(height(node.left), height(node.right))
    }

    private fun balanceFactor(node: AvlNode<K, V>?): Int {
        return if (node == null) 0 else height(node.left) - height(node.right)
    }

    private fun minNode(node: AvlNode<K, V>): AvlNode<K, V> {
        var current: AvlNode<K, V> = node
        while (true) {
            val left = current.left ?: return current
            current = left
        }
    }

    private fun rotateRight(node: AvlNode<K, V>): AvlNode<K, V> {
        val newRoot: AvlNode<K, V> = node.left ?: return node
        val temp = newRoot.right
        newRoot.right = node
        node.left = temp
        updateHeight(node)
        updateHeight(newRoot)
        return newRoot
    }

    private fun rotateLeft(node: AvlNode<K, V>): AvlNode<K, V> {
        val newRoot : AvlNode<K, V> = node.right ?: return node
        val temp = newRoot.left
        newRoot.left = node
        node.right = temp
        updateHeight(node)
        updateHeight(newRoot)
        return newRoot
    }

    private fun rotateRightLeft(node: AvlNode<K, V>): AvlNode<K, V> {
        node.right = node.right?.let { rotateRight(it) }
        return rotateLeft(node)
    }

    private fun rotateLeftRight(node: AvlNode<K, V>): AvlNode<K, V> {
        node.left = node.left?.let { rotateLeft(it) }
        return rotateRight(node)
    }

    private fun balance(node: AvlNode<K, V>): AvlNode<K, V> {
        updateHeight(node)
        val balance = balanceFactor(node)

        if (balance > 1) {
            if (balanceFactor(node.left) >= 0) return rotateRight(node)
            return rotateLeftRight(node)

        }

        if (balance < -1) {
            if (balanceFactor(node.right) <= 0) return rotateLeft(node)
            return rotateRightLeft(node)
        }

        return node
    }

    override fun search(key: K): V? {
        val target = searchNode(root, key)
        if (target != null) return target.value
        return null
    }

    private fun searchNode(node: AvlNode<K, V>?, key: K): AvlNode<K, V>? {
        if (node == null || node.key == key) return node
        if (node.key < key) return searchNode(node.right, key)
        return searchNode(node.left, key)
    }

    override fun insert(key: K, value: V) {
        root = insertNode(root, key, value)
    }

    private fun insertNode(node: AvlNode<K, V>?, key: K, value: V): AvlNode<K, V> {
        if (node == null) {
            size++
            return AvlNode(key, value)
        }
        if (key < node.key) {
            node.left = insertNode(node.left, key, value)
        } else if (key > node.key) {
            node.right = insertNode(node.right, key, value)
        } else {
            node.value = value
            return node
        }
        return balance(node)
    }

    override fun delete(key: K) {
        root = deleteNode(root, key)
    }

    private fun deleteNode(node: AvlNode<K, V>?, key: K): AvlNode<K, V>? {
        if (node == null) return null
        if (key < node.key) {
            node.left = deleteNode(node.left, key)
        } else if (key > node.key) {
            node.right = deleteNode(node.right, key)
        } else {
            if (node.left == null) {
                size--
                return node.right
            } else if (node.right == null) {
                size--
                return node.left
            }
            node.right?.let { right ->
                val temp = minNode(right)
                node.key = temp.key
                node.value = temp.value
                node.right = deleteNode(node.right, temp.key)
            } ?: error("Right  child should not be null")
        }
        return balance(node)
    }

    override fun iterator(): Iterator<Pair<K, V>> {
        return bfsSequence().iterator()
    }

    private fun bfsSequence(): Sequence<Pair<K, V>> = sequence {
        val queue = ArrayDeque<AvlNode<K, V>>()
        root?.let { queue.add(it) }
        while (queue.isNotEmpty()) {
            val node = queue.removeFirst()
            yield(node.key to node.value)
            node.left?.let { queue.add(it) }
            node.right?.let { queue.add(it) }
        }
    }
}
class AvlNode<K : Comparable<K>, V>(
    key: K,
    value: V,
    left: AvlNode<K, V>? = null,
    right: AvlNode<K, V>? = null,
    var height: Int = 1
) : Node<K, V, AvlNode<K, V>>(key, value, left, right)

class AvlTree<K : Comparable<K>, V> : Tree<K, V> {
    private var root: AvlNode<K, V>? = null
    var size = 0

    private fun height(node: AvlNode<K, V>?): Int {
        return node?.height ?: 0
    }

    private fun updateHeight(node: AvlNode<K, V>?) {
        node?.height = 1 + maxOf(height(node.left), height(node.right))
    }

    private fun balanceFactor(node: AvlNode<K, V>?): Int {
        return if (node == null) 0 else height(node.left) - height(node.right)
    }

    private fun minNode(node: AvlNode<K, V>): AvlNode<K, V> {
        var current: AvlNode<K, V> = node
        while (true) {
            val left = current.left ?: return current
            current = left
        }
    }

    private fun rotateRight(node: AvlNode<K, V>): AvlNode<K, V> {
        val newRoot: AvlNode<K, V> = node.left ?: return node
        val temp = newRoot.right
        newRoot.right = node
        node.left = temp
        updateHeight(node)
        updateHeight(newRoot)
        return newRoot
    }

    private fun rotateLeft(node: AvlNode<K, V>): AvlNode<K, V> {
        val newRoot : AvlNode<K, V> = node.right ?: return node
        val temp = newRoot.left
        newRoot.left = node
        node.right = temp
        updateHeight(node)
        updateHeight(newRoot)
        return newRoot
    }

    private fun rotateRightLeft(node: AvlNode<K, V>): AvlNode<K, V> {
        node.right = node.right?.let { rotateRight(it) }
        return rotateLeft(node)
    }

    private fun rotateLeftRight(node: AvlNode<K, V>): AvlNode<K, V> {
        node.left = node.left?.let { rotateLeft(it) }
        return rotateRight(node)
    }

    private fun balance(node: AvlNode<K, V>): AvlNode<K, V> {
        updateHeight(node)
        val balance = balanceFactor(node)

        if (balance > 1) {
            if (balanceFactor(node.left) >= 0) return rotateRight(node)
            return rotateLeftRight(node)

        }

        if (balance < -1) {
            if (balanceFactor(node.right) <= 0) return rotateLeft(node)
            return rotateRightLeft(node)
        }

        return node
    }

    override fun search(key: K): V? {
        val target = searchNode(root, key)
        if (target != null) return target.value
        return null
    }

    private fun searchNode(node: AvlNode<K, V>?, key: K): AvlNode<K, V>? {
        if (node == null || node.key == key) return node
        if (node.key < key) return searchNode(node.right, key)
        return searchNode(node.left, key)
    }

    override fun insert(key: K, value: V) {
        root = insertNode(root, key, value)
    }

    private fun insertNode(node: AvlNode<K, V>?, key: K, value: V): AvlNode<K, V> {
        if (node == null) {
            size++
            return AvlNode(key, value)
        }
        if (key < node.key) {
            node.left = insertNode(node.left, key, value)
        } else if (key > node.key) {
            node.right = insertNode(node.right, key, value)
        } else {
            node.value = value
            return node
        }
        return balance(node)
    }

    override fun delete(key: K) {
        root = deleteNode(root, key)
    }

    private fun deleteNode(node: AvlNode<K, V>?, key: K): AvlNode<K, V>? {
        if (node == null) return null
        if (key < node.key) {
            node.left = deleteNode(node.left, key)
        } else if (key > node.key) {
            node.right = deleteNode(node.right, key)
        } else {
            if (node.left == null) {
                size--
                return node.right
            } else if (node.right == null) {
                size--
                return node.left
            }
            node.right?.let { right ->
                val temp = minNode(right)
                node.key = temp.key
                node.value = temp.value
                node.right = deleteNode(node.right, temp.key)
            } ?: error("Right  child should not be null")
        }
        return balance(node)
    }

    override fun iterator(): Iterator<Pair<K, V>> {
        return bfsSequence().iterator()
    }

    private fun bfsSequence(): Sequence<Pair<K, V>> = sequence {
        val queue = ArrayDeque<AvlNode<K, V>>()
        root?.let { queue.add(it) }
        while (queue.isNotEmpty()) {
            val node = queue.removeFirst()
            yield(node.key to node.value)
            node.left?.let { queue.add(it) }
            node.right?.let { queue.add(it) }
        }
    }
}
class BinNode<K : Comparable<K>, V>(
    key: K,
    value: V,
    left: BinNode<K, V>? = null,
    right: BinNode<K, V>? = null
) : Node<K, V, BinNode<K, V>>(key, value, left, right)

class BinTree<K : Comparable<K>, V> : Tree<K, V> {
    private var root: BinNode<K, V>? = null

    override fun insert(key: K, value: V) {
        if (root == null) {
            root = BinNode(key, value)
            return
        }

        var current = root

        while (current != null) {
            when {
                key < current.key -> {
                    if (current.left == null) {
                        current.left = BinNode(key, value)
                        return
                    }
                    current = current.left
                }

                key > current.key -> {
                    if (current.right == null) {
                        current.right = BinNode(key, value)
                        return
                    }
                    current = current.right
                }

                else -> {
                    current.value = value
                    return
                }
            }
        }
    }

    override fun delete(key: K) {
        root = deleteNode(root, key)
    }

    private fun deleteNode(node: BinNode<K, V>?, key: K): BinNode<K, V>? {
        node ?: return null

        when {
            key < node.key -> node.left = deleteNode(node.left, key)
            key > node.key -> node.right = deleteNode(node.right, key)
            else -> {
                if (node.left == null && node.right == null) {
                    return null
                }
                if (node.left == null) {
                    return node.right
                }
                if (node.right == null) {
                    return node.left
                }

                val rightChild = node.right ?: return node
                val minNode = findMin(rightChild)
                node.key = minNode.key
                node.value = minNode.value
                node.right = deleteNode(node.right, minNode.key)
            }
        }
        return node
    }

    private fun findMin(node: BinNode<K, V>): BinNode<K, V> {
        var current = node
        while (true) {
            val leftChild = current.left ?: break
            current = leftChild
        }
        return current
    }

    override fun search(key: K): V? {
        var current = root

        while (current != null) {
            when {
                key < current.key -> current = current.left
                key > current.key -> current = current.right
                else -> return current.value
            }
        }

        return null
    }

    override fun iterator(): Iterator<Pair<K, V>> {
        return bfsSequence().iterator()
    }

    private fun bfsSequence(): Sequence<Pair<K, V>> = sequence {
        val queue = ArrayDeque<BinNode<K, V>>()
        root?.let { queue.add(it) }

        while (queue.isNotEmpty()) {
            val node = queue.removeFirst()
            yield(node.key to node.value)
            node.left?.let { queue.add(it) }
            node.right?.let { queue.add(it) }
        }
    }
}class BinNode<K : Comparable<K>, V>(
    key: K,
    value: V,
    left: BinNode<K, V>? = null,
    right: BinNode<K, V>? = null
) : Node<K, V, BinNode<K, V>>(key, value, left, right)

class BinTree<K : Comparable<K>, V> : Tree<K, V> {
    private var root: BinNode<K, V>? = null

    override fun insert(key: K, value: V) {
        if (root == null) {
            root = BinNode(key, value)
            return
        }

        var current = root

        while (current != null) {
            when {
                key < current.key -> {
                    if (current.left == null) {
                        current.left = BinNode(key, value)
                        return
                    }
                    current = current.left
                }

                key > current.key -> {
                    if (current.right == null) {
                        current.right = BinNode(key, value)
                        return
                    }
                    current = current.right
                }

                else -> {
                    current.value = value
                    return
                }
            }
        }
    }

    override fun delete(key: K) {
        root = deleteNode(root, key)
    }

    private fun deleteNode(node: BinNode<K, V>?, key: K): BinNode<K, V>? {
        node ?: return null

        when {
            key < node.key -> node.left = deleteNode(node.left, key)
            key > node.key -> node.right = deleteNode(node.right, key)
            else -> {
                if (node.left == null && node.right == null) {
                    return null
                }
                if (node.left == null) {
                    return node.right
                }
                if (node.right == null) {
                    return node.left
                }

                val rightChild = node.right ?: return node
                val minNode = findMin(rightChild)
                node.key = minNode.key
                node.value = minNode.value
                node.right = deleteNode(node.right, minNode.key)
            }
        }
        return node
    }

    private fun findMin(node: BinNode<K, V>): BinNode<K, V> {
        var current = node
        while (true) {
            val leftChild = current.left ?: break
            current = leftChild
        }
        return current
    }

    override fun search(key: K): V? {
        var current = root

        while (current != null) {
            when {
                key < current.key -> current = current.left
                key > current.key -> current = current.right
                else -> return current.value
            }
        }

        return null
    }

    override fun iterator(): Iterator<Pair<K, V>> {
        return bfsSequence().iterator()
    }

    private fun bfsSequence(): Sequence<Pair<K, V>> = sequence {
        val queue = ArrayDeque<BinNode<K, V>>()
        root?.let { queue.add(it) }

        while (queue.isNotEmpty()) {
            val node = queue.removeFirst()
            yield(node.key to node.value)
            node.left?.let { queue.add(it) }
            node.right?.let { queue.add(it) }
        }
    }
}abstract class Node<K : Comparable<K>, V, N : Node<K, V, N>>(
    var key : K,
    var value : V,
    var left: N? = null,
    var right: N? = null
)

interface Tree<K : Comparable<K>, V> : Iterable<Pair<K, V>> {
    fun insert(key: K, value: V)
    fun delete(key: K)
    fun search(key: K): V?
}
abstract class Node<K : Comparable<K>, V, N : Node<K, V, N>>(
    var key : K,
    var value : V,
    var left: N? = null,
    var right: N? = null
)

interface Tree<K : Comparable<K>, V> : Iterable<Pair<K, V>> {
    fun insert(key: K, value: V)
    fun delete(key: K)
    fun search(key: K): V?
}

enum class NodeColor {
    RED, BLACK
}

class RBNode<K: Comparable<K>, V>(
    key: K,
    value: V,
    left: RBNode<K, V>? = null,
    right: RBNode<K, V>? = null,
    var parent: RBNode<K, V>? = null,
    var color: NodeColor = NodeColor.RED,
): Node<K, V, RBNode<K, V>>(key, value, left, right)

class RBTree<K: Comparable<K>, V>: Tree<K, V> {
    private var root: RBNode<K, V>? = null

    override fun insert(key: K, value: V) {
        val newNode = RBNode(key, value)

        if (root == null) {
            root = newNode
        } else {
            insertBST(root, newNode)
        }

        fixAfterInsert(newNode)
    }

    override fun delete(key: K) {
        val node = findNode(key) ?: return
        deleteNode(node)
    }

    override fun search(key: K): V? {
        val node = findNode(key)
        return node?.value
    }

    override fun iterator(): Iterator<Pair<K, V>> {
        return bfsSequence().iterator()
    }

    private fun insertBST(current: RBNode<K, V>?, node: RBNode<K, V>) {
        if (current != null) {
            when {
                node.key < current.key -> {
                    val currentLeftChild = current.left

                    if (currentLeftChild == null) {
                        current.left = node
                        node.parent = current
                    } else {
                        insertBST(currentLeftChild, node)
                    }
                }

                node.key > current.key -> {
                    val currentRightChild = current.right

                    if (currentRightChild == null) {
                        current.right = node
                        node.parent = current
                    } else {
                        insertBST(currentRightChild, node)
                    }
                }

                else -> {
                    current.value = node.value
                }
            }
        }
    }

    private fun deleteNode(node: RBNode<K, V>?) {
        var y = node
        var yOriginalColor = y?.color
        var x: RBNode<K, V>?

        if (node?.left == null) {
            x = node?.right
            transplant(node, node?.right)
        } else if (node.right == null) {                        
            x = node.left
            transplant(node, node.left)
        } else {
            y = minimum(node.right)
            yOriginalColor = y?.color
            x = y?.right

            if (y?.parent == node) {
                x?.parent = y
            } else {
                transplant(y, y?.right)
                y?.right = node.right
                y?.right?.parent = y
            }

            transplant(node, y)
            y?.left = node.left
            y?.left?.parent = y
            y?.color = node.color
        }

        if (yOriginalColor == NodeColor.BLACK) {
            fixAfterDelete(x)
        }
    }

    private fun findNode(key: K): RBNode<K, V>? {
        var current = root

        while (current != null) {
            current = when {
                key > current.key -> current.right
                key < current.key -> current.left
                else -> return current
            }
        }

        return null
    }

    private fun rotateLeft(x: RBNode<K, V>?) {         //x        y
        val y = x?.right ?: return                     // \  ->  /
                                                       //  y    x
        x.right = y.left
        y.left?.parent = x

        val parent = x.parent
        y.parent = parent

        when {
            parent == null -> root = y
            x == parent.left -> parent.left = y
            else -> parent.right = y
        }

        y.left = x
        x.parent = y
    }

    private fun rotateRight(x: RBNode<K, V>?) {        // x     y
        val y = x?.left ?: return                     // /  ->   \
                                                     // y         x
        x.left = y.right
        y.right?.parent = x

        val parent = x.parent
        y.parent = parent

        when {
            parent == null -> root = y
            x == parent.right -> parent.right = y
            else -> parent.left = y
        }

        y.right = x
        x.parent = y
    }

    private fun fixAfterInsert(node: RBNode<K, V>) {
        var current: RBNode<K, V>? = node

        while (current != root && current?.parent?.color == NodeColor.RED) {
            val grandparent = current.parent?.parent

            if (current.parent == grandparent?.left) {
                val uncle = grandparent?.right

                if (uncle?.color == NodeColor.RED) {
                    current.parent?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    uncle.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    grandparent.color = NodeColor.RED
                    current = grandparent
                } else {
                    if (current == current.parent?.right) {
                        val parent = current.parent

                        if (parent != null) {
                            current = parent
                            rotateLeft(current)
                        }
                    }

                    current.parent?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    grandparent?.color = NodeColor.RED
                    rotateRight(grandparent)
                }
            } else {
                val uncle = grandparent?.left

                if (uncle?.color == NodeColor.RED) {
                    current.parent?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    uncle.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    grandparent.color = NodeColor.RED
                    current = grandparent
                } else {
                    if (current == current.parent?.left) {
                        current = current.parent
                        rotateRight(current)
                    }

                    current?.parent?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    grandparent?.color = NodeColor.RED
                    rotateLeft(grandparent)
                }
            }
        }

        root?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
    }

    private fun minimum(node: RBNode<K, V>?): RBNode<K, V>? {
        var current = node

        while (current?.left != null) {
            current = current.left
        }

        return current
    }

    private fun transplant(x: RBNode<K, V>?, y: RBNode<K, V>?) {
        when {
            x?.parent == null -> root = y                   //   P
            x == x.parent?.left -> x.parent?.left = y       //  /            P
            else -> x.parent?.right = y                     // x      ->    /
        }                                                  // / \          y
                                                          // L   R
        y?.parent = x?.parent
    }

    private fun fixAfterDelete(node: RBNode<K, V>?) {
        var current = node

        while (current != root && current?.color != NodeColor.BLACK) {
            val parent = current?.parent ?: break

            if (current == parent.left) {
                var brother = parent.right

                if (brother?.color == NodeColor.RED) {
                    brother.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    parent.color = NodeColor.RED
                    rotateLeft(parent)
                    brother = parent.right
                } else {
                    if (brother?.left?.color == NodeColor.BLACK && brother.right?.color == NodeColor.BLACK) {
                        brother.color = NodeColor.RED
                        current = parent
                    } else {
                        if (brother?.right?.color == NodeColor.BLACK) {
                            brother.left?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                            brother.color = NodeColor.RED
                            rotateRight(brother)
                            brother = parent.right
                        }

                        brother?.color = parent.color
                        parent.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                        brother?.right?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                        rotateLeft(parent)
                        current = root
                    }
                }
            } else {
                var brother = parent.left

                if (brother?.color == NodeColor.RED) {
                    brother.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    parent.color = NodeColor.RED
                    rotateRight(parent)
                    brother = parent.left
                } else {
                    if (brother?.left?.color == NodeColor.BLACK && brother.right?.color == NodeColor.BLACK) {
                        brother.color = NodeColor.RED
                        current = parent
                    } else {
                        if (brother?.left?.color == NodeColor.BLACK) {
                            brother.right?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                            brother.color = NodeColor.RED
                            rotateLeft(brother)
                            brother = parent.left
                        }

                        brother?.color = parent.color
                        parent.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                        brother?.left?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                        rotateRight(parent)
                        current = root
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        current?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
    }

    private fun bfsSequence(): Sequence<Pair<K, V>> = sequence {
        val queue = ArrayDeque<RBNode<K, V>>()
        root?.let { queue.add(it) }

        while (queue.isNotEmpty()) {
            val node = queue.removeFirst()
            yield(node.key to node.value)
            node.left?.let { queue.add(it) }
            node.right?.let { queue.add(it) }
        }
    }
}

enum class NodeColor {
    RED, BLACK
}

class RBNode<K: Comparable<K>, V>(
    key: K,
    value: V,
    left: RBNode<K, V>? = null,
    right: RBNode<K, V>? = null,
    var parent: RBNode<K, V>? = null,
    var color: NodeColor = NodeColor.RED,
): Node<K, V, RBNode<K, V>>(key, value, left, right)

class RBTree<K: Comparable<K>, V>: Tree<K, V> {
    private var root: RBNode<K, V>? = null

    override fun insert(key: K, value: V) {
        val newNode = RBNode(key, value)

        if (root == null) {
            root = newNode
        } else {
            insertBST(root, newNode)
        }

        fixAfterInsert(newNode)
    }

    override fun delete(key: K) {
        val node = findNode(key) ?: return
        deleteNode(node)
    }

    override fun search(key: K): V? {
        val node = findNode(key)
        return node?.value
    }

    override fun iterator(): Iterator<Pair<K, V>> {
        return bfsSequence().iterator()
    }

    private fun insertBST(current: RBNode<K, V>?, node: RBNode<K, V>) {
        if (current != null) {
            when {
                node.key < current.key -> {
                    val currentLeftChild = current.left

                    if (currentLeftChild == null) {
                        current.left = node
                        node.parent = current
                    } else {
                        insertBST(currentLeftChild, node)
                    }
                }

                node.key > current.key -> {
                    val currentRightChild = current.right

                    if (currentRightChild == null) {
                        current.right = node
                        node.parent = current
                    } else {
                        insertBST(currentRightChild, node)
                    }
                }

                else -> {
                    current.value = node.value
                }
            }
        }
    }

    private fun deleteNode(node: RBNode<K, V>?) {
        var y = node
        var yOriginalColor = y?.color
        var x: RBNode<K, V>?

        if (node?.left == null) {
            x = node?.right
            transplant(node, node?.right)
        } else if (node.right == null) {                        
            x = node.left
            transplant(node, node.left)
        } else {
            y = minimum(node.right)
            yOriginalColor = y?.color
            x = y?.right

            if (y?.parent == node) {
                x?.parent = y
            } else {
                transplant(y, y?.right)
                y?.right = node.right
                y?.right?.parent = y
            }

            transplant(node, y)
            y?.left = node.left
            y?.left?.parent = y
            y?.color = node.color
        }

        if (yOriginalColor == NodeColor.BLACK) {
            fixAfterDelete(x)
        }
    }

    private fun findNode(key: K): RBNode<K, V>? {
        var current = root

        while (current != null) {
            current = when {
                key > current.key -> current.right
                key < current.key -> current.left
                else -> return current
            }
        }

        return null
    }

    private fun rotateLeft(x: RBNode<K, V>?) {         //x        y
        val y = x?.right ?: return                     // \  ->  /
                                                       //  y    x
        x.right = y.left
        y.left?.parent = x

        val parent = x.parent
        y.parent = parent

        when {
            parent == null -> root = y
            x == parent.left -> parent.left = y
            else -> parent.right = y
        }

        y.left = x
        x.parent = y
    }

    private fun rotateRight(x: RBNode<K, V>?) {        // x     y
        val y = x?.left ?: return                     // /  ->   \
                                                     // y         x
        x.left = y.right
        y.right?.parent = x

        val parent = x.parent
        y.parent = parent

        when {
            parent == null -> root = y
            x == parent.right -> parent.right = y
            else -> parent.left = y
        }

        y.right = x
        x.parent = y
    }

    private fun fixAfterInsert(node: RBNode<K, V>) {
        var current: RBNode<K, V>? = node

        while (current != root && current?.parent?.color == NodeColor.RED) {
            val grandparent = current.parent?.parent

            if (current.parent == grandparent?.left) {
                val uncle = grandparent?.right

                if (uncle?.color == NodeColor.RED) {
                    current.parent?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    uncle.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    grandparent.color = NodeColor.RED
                    current = grandparent
                } else {
                    if (current == current.parent?.right) {
                        val parent = current.parent

                        if (parent != null) {
                            current = parent
                            rotateLeft(current)
                        }
                    }

                    current.parent?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    grandparent?.color = NodeColor.RED
                    rotateRight(grandparent)
                }
            } else {
                val uncle = grandparent?.left

                if (uncle?.color == NodeColor.RED) {
                    current.parent?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    uncle.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    grandparent.color = NodeColor.RED
                    current = grandparent
                } else {
                    if (current == current.parent?.left) {
                        current = current.parent
                        rotateRight(current)
                    }

                    current?.parent?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    grandparent?.color = NodeColor.RED
                    rotateLeft(grandparent)
                }
            }
        }

        root?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
    }

    private fun minimum(node: RBNode<K, V>?): RBNode<K, V>? {
        var current = node

        while (current?.left != null) {
            current = current.left
        }

        return current
    }

    private fun transplant(x: RBNode<K, V>?, y: RBNode<K, V>?) {
        when {
            x?.parent == null -> root = y                   //   P
            x == x.parent?.left -> x.parent?.left = y       //  /            P
            else -> x.parent?.right = y                     // x      ->    /
        }                                                  // / \          y
                                                          // L   R
        y?.parent = x?.parent
    }

    private fun fixAfterDelete(node: RBNode<K, V>?) {
        var current = node

        while (current != root && current?.color != NodeColor.BLACK) {
            val parent = current?.parent ?: break

            if (current == parent.left) {
                var brother = parent.right

                if (brother?.color == NodeColor.RED) {
                    brother.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    parent.color = NodeColor.RED
                    rotateLeft(parent)
                    brother = parent.right
                } else {
                    if (brother?.left?.color == NodeColor.BLACK && brother.right?.color == NodeColor.BLACK) {
                        brother.color = NodeColor.RED
                        current = parent
                    } else {
                        if (brother?.right?.color == NodeColor.BLACK) {
                            brother.left?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                            brother.color = NodeColor.RED
                            rotateRight(brother)
                            brother = parent.right
                        }

                        brother?.color = parent.color
                        parent.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                        brother?.right?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                        rotateLeft(parent)
                        current = root
                    }
                }
            } else {
                var brother = parent.left

                if (brother?.color == NodeColor.RED) {
                    brother.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                    parent.color = NodeColor.RED
                    rotateRight(parent)
                    brother = parent.left
                } else {
                    if (brother?.left?.color == NodeColor.BLACK && brother.right?.color == NodeColor.BLACK) {
                        brother.color = NodeColor.RED
                        current = parent
                    } else {
                        if (brother?.left?.color == NodeColor.BLACK) {
                            brother.right?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                            brother.color = NodeColor.RED
                            rotateLeft(brother)
                            brother = parent.left
                        }

                        brother?.color = parent.color
                        parent.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                        brother?.left?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
                        rotateRight(parent)
                        current = root
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        current?.color = NodeColor.BLACK
    }

    private fun bfsSequence(): Sequence<Pair<K, V>> = sequence {
        val queue = ArrayDeque<RBNode<K, V>>()
        root?.let { queue.add(it) }

        while (queue.isNotEmpty()) {
            val node = queue.removeFirst()
            yield(node.key to node.value)
            node.left?.let { queue.add(it) }
            node.right?.let { queue.add(it) }
        }
    }
}
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.assertEquals
import org.junit.jupiter.api.BeforeEach
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test

class AvlTreeTest {

    private lateinit var tree: AvlTree<Int, String>

    @BeforeEach
    fun setup() {
        tree = AvlTree()
    }

    @Test
    fun emptyTree() {
        assertEquals(0, tree.size)
        assertEquals(false, tree.iterator().hasNext())
    }

    @Test
    fun insertElement() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        val expectedList = listOf(5 to "five")
        assertEquals(1, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun insertExistingElement() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(5, "new_five")

        val expectedList = listOf(5 to "new_five")

        assertEquals(1, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun searchElementInSingleNodeTree() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")

        assertEquals("five", tree.search(5))
    }

    @Test
    fun insertMultipleElements1() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(3, "three")

        val expectedList = listOf(
            5 to "five",
            3 to "three",
            7 to "seven"
        )

        assertEquals(3, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun searchNonExistingElement() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(3, "three")

        assertEquals(null, tree.search(4))
    }

    @Test
    fun insertMultipleElements2() {
        tree.insert(4, "four")
        tree.insert(6, "six")
        tree.insert(2, "two")
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(1, "one")

        val expectedList = listOf(
            4 to "four",
            2 to "two",
            6 to "six",
            1 to "one",
            3 to "three",
            5 to "five",
            7 to "seven"
        )

        assertEquals(7, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun searchMultipleElements() {
        tree.insert(4, "four")
        tree.insert(6, "six")
        tree.insert(2, "two")
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(1, "one")

        assertEquals("four", tree.search(4))
        assertEquals("six", tree.search(6))
        assertEquals("two", tree.search(2))
        assertEquals("five", tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("three", tree.search(3))
        assertEquals("seven", tree.search(7))
        assertEquals("one", tree.search(1))
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteLeafElement() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.delete(7)

        val expectedList = listOf(
            5 to "five",
            3 to "three"
        )

        assertEquals(2, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun insertRightRotation() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(1, "one")
        tree.insert(13, "thirteen")
        tree.insert(2, "two")
        tree.insert(3, "three")

        val expectedList = listOf(
            5 to "five",
            2 to "two",
            7 to "seven",
            1 to "one",
            3 to "three",
            13 to "thirteen"
        )

        assertEquals(6, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun insertRightLeftRotation() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(1, "one")
        tree.insert(13, "thirteen")
        tree.insert(2, "two")
        tree.insert(11, "eleven")

        val expectedList = listOf(
            5 to "five",
            1 to "one",
            11 to "eleven",
            2 to "two",
            7 to "seven",
            13 to "thirteen"
        )

        assertEquals(6, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun insertLeftRotation() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(2, "two")
        tree.insert(8, "eight")
        tree.insert(1, "one")

        val expectedList = listOf(
            5 to "five",
            2 to "two",
            7 to "seven",
            1 to "one",
            3 to "three",
            8 to "eight"
        )

        assertEquals(6, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun insertLeftRightRotation() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(1, "one")
        tree.insert(8, "eight")
        tree.insert(2, "two")

        val expectedList = listOf(
            5 to "five",
            2 to "two",
            7 to "seven",
            1 to "one",
            3 to "three",
            8 to "eight"
        )

        assertEquals(6, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteElementWithOnlyLeftChild() {
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(9, "nine")
        tree.insert(4, "four")
        tree.insert(8, "eight")
        tree.insert(2, "two")

        tree.delete(4)

        val expectedList = listOf(
            7 to "seven",
            2 to "two",
            9 to "nine",
            8 to "eight"
        )

        assertEquals(4, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteElementWithOnlyRightChild() {
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(9, "nine")
        tree.insert(4, "four")
        tree.insert(8, "eight")
        tree.insert(6, "six")

        tree.delete(4)

        val expectedList = listOf(
            7 to "seven",
            6 to "six",
            9 to "nine",
            8 to "eight"
        )

        assertEquals(4, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteElementWithTwoChildren() {
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(9, "nine")
        tree.insert(4, "four")
        tree.insert(8, "eight")
        tree.insert(2, "two")
        tree.insert(10, "ten")
        tree.insert(6, "six")
        tree.insert(1, "one")
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")

        tree.delete(4)

        val expectedList = listOf(
            7 to "seven",
            5 to "five",
            9 to "nine",
            2 to "two",
            6 to "six",
            8 to "eight",
            10 to "ten",
            1 to "one",
            3 to "three"
        )

        assertEquals(9, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }
}
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.assertEquals
import org.junit.jupiter.api.BeforeEach
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test

class AvlTreeTest {

    private lateinit var tree: AvlTree<Int, String>

    @BeforeEach
    fun setup() {
        tree = AvlTree()
    }

    @Test
    fun emptyTree() {
        assertEquals(0, tree.size)
        assertEquals(false, tree.iterator().hasNext())
    }

    @Test
    fun insertElement() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        val expectedList = listOf(5 to "five")
        assertEquals(1, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun insertExistingElement() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(5, "new_five")

        val expectedList = listOf(5 to "new_five")

        assertEquals(1, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun searchElementInSingleNodeTree() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")

        assertEquals("five", tree.search(5))
    }

    @Test
    fun insertMultipleElements1() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(3, "three")

        val expectedList = listOf(
            5 to "five",
            3 to "three",
            7 to "seven"
        )

        assertEquals(3, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun searchNonExistingElement() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(3, "three")

        assertEquals(null, tree.search(4))
    }

    @Test
    fun insertMultipleElements2() {
        tree.insert(4, "four")
        tree.insert(6, "six")
        tree.insert(2, "two")
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(1, "one")

        val expectedList = listOf(
            4 to "four",
            2 to "two",
            6 to "six",
            1 to "one",
            3 to "three",
            5 to "five",
            7 to "seven"
        )

        assertEquals(7, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun searchMultipleElements() {
        tree.insert(4, "four")
        tree.insert(6, "six")
        tree.insert(2, "two")
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(1, "one")

        assertEquals("four", tree.search(4))
        assertEquals("six", tree.search(6))
        assertEquals("two", tree.search(2))
        assertEquals("five", tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("three", tree.search(3))
        assertEquals("seven", tree.search(7))
        assertEquals("one", tree.search(1))
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteLeafElement() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.delete(7)

        val expectedList = listOf(
            5 to "five",
            3 to "three"
        )

        assertEquals(2, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun insertRightRotation() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(1, "one")
        tree.insert(13, "thirteen")
        tree.insert(2, "two")
        tree.insert(3, "three")

        val expectedList = listOf(
            5 to "five",
            2 to "two",
            7 to "seven",
            1 to "one",
            3 to "three",
            13 to "thirteen"
        )

        assertEquals(6, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun insertRightLeftRotation() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(1, "one")
        tree.insert(13, "thirteen")
        tree.insert(2, "two")
        tree.insert(11, "eleven")

        val expectedList = listOf(
            5 to "five",
            1 to "one",
            11 to "eleven",
            2 to "two",
            7 to "seven",
            13 to "thirteen"
        )

        assertEquals(6, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun insertLeftRotation() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(2, "two")
        tree.insert(8, "eight")
        tree.insert(1, "one")

        val expectedList = listOf(
            5 to "five",
            2 to "two",
            7 to "seven",
            1 to "one",
            3 to "three",
            8 to "eight"
        )

        assertEquals(6, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun insertLeftRightRotation() {
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(1, "one")
        tree.insert(8, "eight")
        tree.insert(2, "two")

        val expectedList = listOf(
            5 to "five",
            2 to "two",
            7 to "seven",
            1 to "one",
            3 to "three",
            8 to "eight"
        )

        assertEquals(6, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteElementWithOnlyLeftChild() {
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(9, "nine")
        tree.insert(4, "four")
        tree.insert(8, "eight")
        tree.insert(2, "two")

        tree.delete(4)

        val expectedList = listOf(
            7 to "seven",
            2 to "two",
            9 to "nine",
            8 to "eight"
        )

        assertEquals(4, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteElementWithOnlyRightChild() {
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(9, "nine")
        tree.insert(4, "four")
        tree.insert(8, "eight")
        tree.insert(6, "six")

        tree.delete(4)

        val expectedList = listOf(
            7 to "seven",
            6 to "six",
            9 to "nine",
            8 to "eight"
        )

        assertEquals(4, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteElementWithTwoChildren() {
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(9, "nine")
        tree.insert(4, "four")
        tree.insert(8, "eight")
        tree.insert(2, "two")
        tree.insert(10, "ten")
        tree.insert(6, "six")
        tree.insert(1, "one")
        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")

        tree.delete(4)

        val expectedList = listOf(
            7 to "seven",
            5 to "five",
            9 to "nine",
            2 to "two",
            6 to "six",
            8 to "eight",
            10 to "ten",
            1 to "one",
            3 to "three"
        )

        assertEquals(9, tree.size)
        assertEquals(expectedList, tree.toList())
    }
}
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.assertEquals
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.assertNull
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.assertTrue

class BinTreeTest {

    @Test
    fun searchInEmptyTreeReturnsNull() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        assertNull(tree.search(10))
    }

    @Test
    fun insertOneElementAndFindIt() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")

        assertEquals("five", tree.search(5))
    }

    @Test
    fun insertSeveralElementsAndFindThem() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")

        assertEquals("five", tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("three", tree.search(3))
        assertEquals("seven", tree.search(7))
    }

    @Test
    fun insertExistingKeyReplacesValue() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "old")
        tree.insert(5, "new")

        assertEquals("new", tree.search(5))
    }

    @Test
    fun searchMissingKeyReturnsNull() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")

        assertNull(tree.search(10))
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteFromEmptyTreeDoesNothing() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.delete(10)

        assertNull(tree.search(10))
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteLeaf() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")

        tree.delete(3)

        assertNull(tree.search(3))
        assertEquals("five", tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("seven", tree.search(7))
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteNodeWithOnlyLeftChild() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(2, "two")

        tree.delete(3)

        assertNull(tree.search(3))
        assertEquals("two", tree.search(2))
        assertEquals("five", tree.search(5))
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteNodeWithOnlyRightChild() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(8, "eight")

        tree.delete(7)

        assertNull(tree.search(7))
        assertEquals("eight", tree.search(8))
        assertEquals("five", tree.search(5))
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteNodeWithTwoChildren() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(6, "six")
        tree.insert(8, "eight")

        tree.delete(7)

        assertNull(tree.search(7))
        assertEquals("six", tree.search(6))
        assertEquals("eight", tree.search(8))
        assertEquals("five", tree.search(5))
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteRoot() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")

        tree.delete(5)

        assertNull(tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("three", tree.search(3))
        assertEquals("seven", tree.search(7))
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteRootWithOneChild() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")

        tree.delete(5)

        assertNull(tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("three", tree.search(3))
    }

    @Test
    fun deleteMissingKeyDoesNothing() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")

        tree.delete(10)

        assertEquals("five", tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("three", tree.search(3))
        assertEquals("seven", tree.search(7))
    }

    @Test
    fun iteratorOnEmptyTree() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        val result = tree.toList()

        assertTrue(result.isEmpty())
    }

    @Test
    fun iteratorReturnsElementsInBFSOrder() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(2, "two")
        tree.insert(4, "four")

        val result = tree.toList()

        assertEquals(
            listOf(
                5 to "five",
                3 to "three",
                7 to "seven",
                2 to "two",
                4 to "four",
            ), result)
    }

    @Test
    fun iteratorWorksCorrectlyAfterDeletion() {
        val tree = BinTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(5, "five")
        tree.insert(3, "three")
        tree.insert(7, "seven")
        tree.insert(6, "six")
        tree.insert(8, "eight")

        tree.delete(7)

        val result = tree.toList()

        assertEquals(
            listOf(
                5 to "five",
                3 to "three",
                8 to "eight",
                6 to "six"
            ), result)
    }
}import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.assertEquals
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.assertNull
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.assertTrue

class BinTreeTest {
