}import org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.*
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test
import kotlin.random.Random

class RBTreeTest {

    @Test
    fun `insert and search`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(10, "A")
        tree.insert(5, "B")
        tree.insert(20, "C")

        assertEquals("A", tree.search(10))
        assertEquals("B", tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("C", tree.search(20))
        assertNull(tree.search(100))
    }

    @Test
    fun `insert duplicate key replaces value`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(10, "A")
        tree.insert(10, "B")

        assertEquals("B", tree.search(10))
    }

    @Test
    fun `bfs iterator returns elements`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(10, "A")
        tree.insert(5, "B")
        tree.insert(20, "C")

        val result = tree.iterator().asSequence().toList()

        assertEquals(3, result.size)
        assertTrue(result.contains(10 to "A"))
        assertTrue(result.contains(5 to "B"))
        assertTrue(result.contains(20 to "C"))
    }

    @Test
    fun `delete leaf node`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(10, "A")
        tree.insert(5, "B")

        tree.delete(5)

        assertNull(tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("A", tree.search(10))
    }

    @Test
    fun `delete node with one child`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(10, "A")
        tree.insert(5, "B")
        tree.insert(3, "C")

        tree.delete(5)

        assertNull(tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("C", tree.search(3))
    }

    @Test
    fun `delete node with two children`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(10, "A")
        tree.insert(5, "B")
        tree.insert(20, "C")
        tree.insert(15, "D")
        tree.insert(30, "E")

        tree.delete(10)

        assertNull(tree.search(10))
        assertEquals("B", tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("C", tree.search(20))
        assertEquals("D", tree.search(15))
    }

    @Test
    fun `delete root`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(10, "A")
        tree.insert(5, "B")
        tree.insert(20, "C")

        tree.delete(10)

        assertNull(tree.search(10))
        assertEquals(2, tree.iterator().asSequence().count())
    }

    @Test
    fun `insert many elements`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, Int>()

        for (i in 1..1000) {
            tree.insert(i, i)
        }

        for (i in 1..1000) {
            assertEquals(i, tree.search(i))
        }
    }

    @Test
    fun `insert and delete many`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, Int>()

        for (i in 1..100) {
            tree.insert(i, i)
        }

        for (i in 1..100) {
            tree.delete(i)
        }

        for (i in 1..100) {
            assertNull(tree.search(i))
        }
    }

    @Test
    fun `random operations`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, Int>()
        val map = mutableMapOf<Int, Int>()

        val keys = (1..100).shuffled()

        for (k in keys) {
            tree.insert(k, k)
            map[k] = k
        }

        for (k in keys.shuffled()) {
            assertEquals(map[k], tree.search(k))
            tree.delete(k)
            map.remove(k)
        }

        for (k in keys) {
            assertNull(tree.search(k))
        }
    }

    @Test
    fun `random insert search`() {
        repeat(1000) {
            val tree = RBTree<Int, Int>()
            val set = mutableSetOf<Int>()

            val size = Random.nextInt(1, 100)

            repeat(size) {
                val key = Random.nextInt(0, 1000)
                tree.insert(key, key)
                set.add(key)
            }

            for (k in set) {
                assertEquals(k, tree.search(k))
            }
        }
    }

    @Test
    fun `random insert delete`() {
        repeat(500) {
            val tree = RBTree<Int, Int>()
            val set = mutableSetOf<Int>()

            val keys = List(Random.nextInt(1, 100)) {
                Random.nextInt(0, 1000)
            }

            for (k in keys) {
                tree.insert(k, k)
                set.add(k)
            }

            for (k in keys.shuffled()) {
                tree.delete(k)
                set.remove(k)

                for (x in set) {
                    assertEquals(x, tree.search(x))
                }
            }

            for (k in keys) {
                assertNull(tree.search(k))
            }
        }
    }

    @Test
    fun `random operations stress test`() {
        repeat(200) {
            val tree = RBTree<Int, Int>()
            val map = mutableMapOf<Int, Int>()

            repeat(200) {
                val key = Random.nextInt(0, 1000)

                if (Random.nextBoolean()) {
                    tree.insert(key, key)
                    map[key] = key
                } else {
                    tree.delete(key)
                    map.remove(key)
                }

                for ((k, v) in map) {
                    assertEquals(v, tree.search(k))
                }
            }
        }
    }
}import org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.*
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test
import kotlin.random.Random

class RBTreeTest {

    @Test
    fun `insert and search`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(10, "A")
        tree.insert(5, "B")
        tree.insert(20, "C")

        assertEquals("A", tree.search(10))
        assertEquals("B", tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("C", tree.search(20))
        assertNull(tree.search(100))
    }

    @Test
    fun `insert duplicate key replaces value`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(10, "A")
        tree.insert(10, "B")

        assertEquals("B", tree.search(10))
    }

    @Test
    fun `bfs iterator returns elements`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(10, "A")
        tree.insert(5, "B")
        tree.insert(20, "C")

        val result = tree.iterator().asSequence().toList()

        assertEquals(3, result.size)
        assertTrue(result.contains(10 to "A"))
        assertTrue(result.contains(5 to "B"))
        assertTrue(result.contains(20 to "C"))
    }

    @Test
    fun `delete leaf node`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(10, "A")
        tree.insert(5, "B")

        tree.delete(5)

        assertNull(tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("A", tree.search(10))
    }

    @Test
    fun `delete node with one child`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(10, "A")
        tree.insert(5, "B")
        tree.insert(3, "C")

        tree.delete(5)

        assertNull(tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("C", tree.search(3))
    }

    @Test
    fun `delete node with two children`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(10, "A")
        tree.insert(5, "B")
        tree.insert(20, "C")
        tree.insert(15, "D")
        tree.insert(30, "E")

        tree.delete(10)

        assertNull(tree.search(10))
        assertEquals("B", tree.search(5))
        assertEquals("C", tree.search(20))
        assertEquals("D", tree.search(15))
    }

    @Test
    fun `delete root`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, String>()

        tree.insert(10, "A")
        tree.insert(5, "B")
        tree.insert(20, "C")

        tree.delete(10)

        assertNull(tree.search(10))
        assertEquals(2, tree.iterator().asSequence().count())
    }

    @Test
    fun `insert many elements`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, Int>()

        for (i in 1..1000) {
            tree.insert(i, i)
        }

        for (i in 1..1000) {
            assertEquals(i, tree.search(i))
        }
    }

    @Test
    fun `insert and delete many`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, Int>()

        for (i in 1..100) {
            tree.insert(i, i)
        }

        for (i in 1..100) {
            tree.delete(i)
        }

        for (i in 1..100) {
            assertNull(tree.search(i))
        }
    }

    @Test
    fun `random operations`() {
        val tree = RBTree<Int, Int>()
        val map = mutableMapOf<Int, Int>()

        val keys = (1..100).shuffled()

        for (k in keys) {
            tree.insert(k, k)
            map[k] = k
        }

        for (k in keys.shuffled()) {
            assertEquals(map[k], tree.search(k))
            tree.delete(k)
            map.remove(k)
        }

        for (k in keys) {
            assertNull(tree.search(k))
        }
    }

    @Test
    fun `random insert search`() {
        repeat(1000) {
            val tree = RBTree<Int, Int>()
            val set = mutableSetOf<Int>()

            val size = Random.nextInt(1, 100)

            repeat(size) {
                val key = Random.nextInt(0, 1000)
                tree.insert(key, key)
                set.add(key)
            }

            for (k in set) {
                assertEquals(k, tree.search(k))
            }
        }
    }

    @Test
    fun `random insert delete`() {
        repeat(500) {
            val tree = RBTree<Int, Int>()
            val set = mutableSetOf<Int>()

            val keys = List(Random.nextInt(1, 100)) {
                Random.nextInt(0, 1000)
            }

            for (k in keys) {
                tree.insert(k, k)
                set.add(k)
            }

            for (k in keys.shuffled()) {
                tree.delete(k)
                set.remove(k)

                for (x in set) {
                    assertEquals(x, tree.search(x))
                }
            }

            for (k in keys) {
                assertNull(tree.search(k))
            }
        }
    }

    @Test
    fun `random operations stress test`() {
        repeat(200) {
            val tree = RBTree<Int, Int>()
            val map = mutableMapOf<Int, Int>()

            repeat(200) {
                val key = Random.nextInt(0, 1000)

                if (Random.nextBoolean()) {
                    tree.insert(key, key)
                    map[key] = key
                } else {
                    tree.delete(key)
                    map.remove(key)
                }

                for ((k, v) in map) {
                    assertEquals(v, tree.search(k))
                }
            }
        }
    }
}#pragma once

#include <stdio.h>
#include <sys/types.h>

#define MAX_MESSAGE_LEN 256

ssize_t read_message(FILE *stream, void *buf);
ssize_t write_message(FILE* stream, const void *buf, size_t nbyte);
#pragma once

#include <stdio.h>
#include <sys/types.h>

#define MAX_MESSAGE_LEN 256

ssize_t read_message(FILE *stream, void *buf);
ssize_t write_message(FILE* stream, const void *buf, size_t nbyte);
#include "protocol.h"
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdint.h>

ssize_t read_message(FILE *stream, void *buf) {
    uint8_t *output = buf;
    size_t bytes_read = 0;

    int reading = 1; //to know when to stop
    uint8_t current_byte = 0;
    int bit_count = 0; //bits in current byte
    int consecutive_ones = 0; //to track when there's 5 times 1 in a row

    int searching = 1;
    uint8_t marker_buffer = 0;
    int marker_bits = 0;
    int leftover_bit_pos = -1;  // Track where we stopped in the current byte
    int leftover_byte = 0;
    int zeros_count = 0;
    int all_bits = 0;

    while (searching) {
        int c = getc(stream);
        if (c == EOF) {
            fprintf(stderr, "Error: EOF while searching for start marker\n");
            return -1;
        }
        for (int bit_pos = 0; bit_pos < 8; bit_pos++) {
            int bit = (c >> (7 - bit_pos)) & 1;
            
            marker_buffer = (marker_buffer << 1) | bit;
            marker_bits++;
            if (bit == 0) {
                zeros_count++;
            }
            
            if (marker_bits > 8) {
                marker_bits = 8;
                marker_buffer &= 0xFF;
            }
            
            if (marker_bits == 8 && marker_buffer == 0x7E) {
                if (zeros_count == 2) {
                    searching = 0;
                    leftover_byte = c;
                    leftover_bit_pos = bit_pos + 1;
                    break;
                }
                else {
                    fprintf(stderr, "Error: 0s before start marker");
                    return -1;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    zeros_count = 0;

    if (leftover_bit_pos != -1 && leftover_bit_pos < 8) {
        for (int bit_pos = leftover_bit_pos; bit_pos < 8; bit_pos++) {
            int bit = (leftover_byte >> (7 - bit_pos)) & 1;
            
            if (consecutive_ones == 5) {
                if (bit == 0) {
                    consecutive_ones = 0;
                    zeros_count++;
                    continue;
                } else {
                    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Empty frame or invalid sequence\n");
                    return -1;
                }
            }
            
            current_byte = (current_byte << 1) | bit;
            bit_count++;
            all_bits++;
            
            if (bit == 1) {
                consecutive_ones++;
            } else {
                consecutive_ones = 0;
                zeros_count++;
            }
            
            if (bit_count == 8) {
                if (bytes_read >= MAX_MESSAGE_LEN) {
                    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Message too long\n");
                    return -1;
                }
                output[bytes_read] = current_byte;
                bytes_read++;
                current_byte = 0;
                bit_count = 0;
            }
        }
    }

    while (reading) {
        int c = getc(stream);
        if (c == EOF) {
            fprintf(stderr, "Error: EOF while reading message\n");
            return -1;
        }
        for (int bit_pos = 0; bit_pos < 8; bit_pos++) {
            int bit = (c >> (7 - bit_pos)) & 1;

            if (consecutive_ones == 5) {
                if (bit == 0){
                    zeros_count++;
                    consecutive_ones = 0;                    
                    continue;
                }
            }
        
            if (consecutive_ones == 6) {
                if (bit == 0 && zeros_count != 0) {
                    reading = 0;
                    bit_count = 0;
                    all_bits -= 7;
                    break;
                } else {
                    fprintf (stderr, "Error: Invalid end marker");
                    return -1;
                }
            }
            current_byte = (current_byte << 1) | bit;
            bit_count++;
            all_bits++;

            if (bit == 1) {
                consecutive_ones++;
            }
            else {
                consecutive_ones = 0;
                zeros_count++;
            }

            if (bit_count == 8) {
                if (bytes_read >= MAX_MESSAGE_LEN) {
                    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Message too long\n");
                    return -1;
                }
                output[bytes_read] = current_byte;
                bytes_read++;
                current_byte = 0;
                bit_count = 0;
            }
        }

    }

    if (zeros_count == 0) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: Invalid sequence or end marker");
        return -1;
    }

    if (all_bits % 8 != 0){
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: Message contains incomplete byte\n");
        return -1;
    }

    if (bit_count != 0) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: Message contains incomplete byte\n");
        return -1;
    }

    return bytes_read;
}

ssize_t write_message(FILE* stream, const void *buf, size_t nbyte) {

    if (buf == NULL && nbyte > 0) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: NULL buffer with non-zero size\n");
        return -1;
    }
    const uint8_t *data = buf;
    size_t bytes_written_to_stream = 0;

    uint8_t current_byte = 0;
    int bit_count = 0;
    int consecutive_ones = 0;

    if (putc(0x7E, stream) == EOF) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: Failed to write start marker\n");
        return -1;
    }
    bytes_written_to_stream++;
    
    for (size_t i = 0; i < nbyte; i++) {
        uint8_t byte = data[i];
        for (int bit_pos = 0; bit_pos < 8; bit_pos++) {
            int bit = (byte >> (7 - bit_pos)) & 1;
            current_byte = (current_byte << 1) | bit;
            bit_count++;

            if (bit == 1) {
                consecutive_ones++;
            }
            else {
                consecutive_ones = 0;
            }
            if (consecutive_ones == 5) {
                if (bit_count == 8) {
                    if (putc(current_byte, stream) == EOF) {
                        fprintf(stderr, "Error: Failed to write byte\n");
                        return -1;
                    }
                    bytes_written_to_stream++;
                    bit_count = 0;
                    current_byte = 0;
                }

                current_byte = (current_byte << 1) | 0;
                bit_count++;
                consecutive_ones = 0;

                if (bit_count == 8) {
                    if (putc(current_byte, stream) == EOF) {
                        fprintf(stderr, "Error: Failed to write byte\n");
                        return -1;
                    }
                
                bytes_written_to_stream++;
                bit_count = 0;
                current_byte = 0;
                }
            }

            if (bit_count == 8) {
                if (putc(current_byte, stream) == EOF) {
                    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Failed to write byte\n");
                    return -1;
                }
                
                bytes_written_to_stream++;
                bit_count = 0;
                current_byte = 0;
            }
        }
    }
    uint8_t end_marker = 0x7E;
    if (bit_count > 0) {
        for (int bit_pos = 0; bit_pos < 8; bit_pos++) {
            int bit = (end_marker >> (7 - bit_pos)) & 1;
            current_byte = (current_byte << 1) | bit;
            bit_count++;
            
            if (bit_count == 8) {
                if (putc(current_byte, stream) == EOF) return -1;
                bytes_written_to_stream++;
                current_byte = 0;
                bit_count = 0;
            }
        }
        
        if (bit_count > 0) {
            current_byte = current_byte << (8 - bit_count);
            current_byte |= (1 << (8 - bit_count)) - 1;
            if (putc(current_byte, stream) == EOF) return -1;
            bytes_written_to_stream++;
        }
    } 
    else {
        if (putc(end_marker, stream) == EOF) return -1;
        bytes_written_to_stream++;
    }

    return nbyte;
}
#include "protocol.h"
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdint.h>

ssize_t read_message(FILE *stream, void *buf) {
    uint8_t *output = buf;
    size_t bytes_read = 0;

    int reading = 1; //to know when to stop
    uint8_t current_byte = 0;
    int bit_count = 0; //bits in current byte
    int consecutive_ones = 0; //to track when there's 5 times 1 in a row

    int searching = 1;
    uint8_t marker_buffer = 0;
    int marker_bits = 0;
    int leftover_bit_pos = -1;  // Track where we stopped in the current byte
    int leftover_byte = 0;
    int zeros_count = 0;
    int all_bits = 0;

    while (searching) {
        int c = getc(stream);
        if (c == EOF) {
            fprintf(stderr, "Error: EOF while searching for start marker\n");
            return -1;
        }
        for (int bit_pos = 0; bit_pos < 8; bit_pos++) {
            int bit = (c >> (7 - bit_pos)) & 1;
            
            marker_buffer = (marker_buffer << 1) | bit;
            marker_bits++;
            if (bit == 0) {
                zeros_count++;
            }
            
            if (marker_bits > 8) {
                marker_bits = 8;
                marker_buffer &= 0xFF;
            }
            
            if (marker_bits == 8 && marker_buffer == 0x7E) {
                if (zeros_count == 2) {
                    searching = 0;
                    leftover_byte = c;
                    leftover_bit_pos = bit_pos + 1;
                    break;
                }
                else {
                    fprintf(stderr, "Error: 0s before start marker");
                    return -1;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    zeros_count = 0;

    if (leftover_bit_pos != -1 && leftover_bit_pos < 8) {
        for (int bit_pos = leftover_bit_pos; bit_pos < 8; bit_pos++) {
            int bit = (leftover_byte >> (7 - bit_pos)) & 1;
            
            if (consecutive_ones == 5) {
                if (bit == 0) {
                    consecutive_ones = 0;
                    zeros_count++;
                    continue;
                } else {
                    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Empty frame or invalid sequence\n");
                    return -1;
                }
            }
            
            current_byte = (current_byte << 1) | bit;
            bit_count++;
            all_bits++;
            
            if (bit == 1) {
                consecutive_ones++;
            } else {
                consecutive_ones = 0;
                zeros_count++;
            }
            
            if (bit_count == 8) {
                if (bytes_read >= MAX_MESSAGE_LEN) {
                    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Message too long\n");
                    return -1;
                }
                output[bytes_read] = current_byte;
                bytes_read++;
                current_byte = 0;
                bit_count = 0;
            }
        }
    }

    while (reading) {
        int c = getc(stream);
        if (c == EOF) {
            fprintf(stderr, "Error: EOF while reading message\n");
            return -1;
        }
        for (int bit_pos = 0; bit_pos < 8; bit_pos++) {
            int bit = (c >> (7 - bit_pos)) & 1;

            if (consecutive_ones == 5) {
                if (bit == 0){
                    zeros_count++;
                    consecutive_ones = 0;                    
                    continue;
                }
            }
        
            if (consecutive_ones == 6) {
                if (bit == 0 && zeros_count != 0) {
                    reading = 0;
                    bit_count = 0;
                    all_bits -= 7;
                    break;
                } else {
                    fprintf (stderr, "Error: Invalid end marker");
                    return -1;
                }
            }
            current_byte = (current_byte << 1) | bit;
            bit_count++;
            all_bits++;

            if (bit == 1) {
                consecutive_ones++;
            }
            else {
                consecutive_ones = 0;
                zeros_count++;
            }

            if (bit_count == 8) {
                if (bytes_read >= MAX_MESSAGE_LEN) {
                    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Message too long\n");
                    return -1;
                }
                output[bytes_read] = current_byte;
                bytes_read++;
                current_byte = 0;
                bit_count = 0;
            }
        }

    }

    if (zeros_count == 0) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: Invalid sequence or end marker");
        return -1;
    }

    if (all_bits % 8 != 0){
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: Message contains incomplete byte\n");
        return -1;
    }

    if (bit_count != 0) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: Message contains incomplete byte\n");
        return -1;
    }

    return bytes_read;
}

ssize_t write_message(FILE* stream, const void *buf, size_t nbyte) {

    if (buf == NULL && nbyte > 0) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: NULL buffer with non-zero size\n");
        return -1;
    }
    const uint8_t *data = buf;
    size_t bytes_written_to_stream = 0;

    uint8_t current_byte = 0;
    int bit_count = 0;
    int consecutive_ones = 0;

    if (putc(0x7E, stream) == EOF) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: Failed to write start marker\n");
        return -1;
    }
    bytes_written_to_stream++;
    
    for (size_t i = 0; i < nbyte; i++) {
        uint8_t byte = data[i];
        for (int bit_pos = 0; bit_pos < 8; bit_pos++) {
            int bit = (byte >> (7 - bit_pos)) & 1;
            current_byte = (current_byte << 1) | bit;
            bit_count++;

            if (bit == 1) {
                consecutive_ones++;
            }
            else {
                consecutive_ones = 0;
            }
            if (consecutive_ones == 5) {
                if (bit_count == 8) {
                    if (putc(current_byte, stream) == EOF) {
                        fprintf(stderr, "Error: Failed to write byte\n");
                        return -1;
                    }
                    bytes_written_to_stream++;
                    bit_count = 0;
                    current_byte = 0;
                }

                current_byte = (current_byte << 1) | 0;
                bit_count++;
                consecutive_ones = 0;

                if (bit_count == 8) {
                    if (putc(current_byte, stream) == EOF) {
                        fprintf(stderr, "Error: Failed to write byte\n");
                        return -1;
                    }
                
                bytes_written_to_stream++;
                bit_count = 0;
                current_byte = 0;
                }
            }

            if (bit_count == 8) {
                if (putc(current_byte, stream) == EOF) {
                    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Failed to write byte\n");
                    return -1;
                }
                
                bytes_written_to_stream++;
                bit_count = 0;
                current_byte = 0;
            }
        }
    }
    uint8_t end_marker = 0x7E;
    if (bit_count > 0) {
        for (int bit_pos = 0; bit_pos < 8; bit_pos++) {
            int bit = (end_marker >> (7 - bit_pos)) & 1;
            current_byte = (current_byte << 1) | bit;
            bit_count++;
            
            if (bit_count == 8) {
                if (putc(current_byte, stream) == EOF) return -1;
                bytes_written_to_stream++;
                current_byte = 0;
                bit_count = 0;
            }
        }
        
        if (bit_count > 0) {
            current_byte = current_byte << (8 - bit_count);
            current_byte |= (1 << (8 - bit_count)) - 1;
            if (putc(current_byte, stream) == EOF) return -1;
            bytes_written_to_stream++;
        }
    } 
    else {
        if (putc(end_marker, stream) == EOF) return -1;
        bytes_written_to_stream++;
    }

    return nbyte;
}
#include "protocol.h"

#include <stdarg.h>
#include <stddef.h>
#include <setjmp.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <memory.h>
#include <inttypes.h>
#include <sys/types.h>

#include <cmocka.h>

#if defined(getc) || defined(putc) || defined(fprintf)
#error "Not handled yet: redefinition of stdio functions"
#endif

#define TEST_BUFFER_SIZE 512
static char buffer_stderr[TEST_BUFFER_SIZE];
static volatile size_t buffer_putc_len;
static uint8_t buffer_putc[TEST_BUFFER_SIZE];
static size_t buffer_getc_len;
static size_t buffer_getc_index;
static uint8_t buffer_getc[TEST_BUFFER_SIZE];

static FILE *message_stream;

static enum {
    UNDEFINED,
    MSB_FIRST,
    LSB_FIRST,
} mode = UNDEFINED;

/**
 * A mock getc function that get character from buffer
 * @param[in] stream
 * @return reads the next character from buffer and returns it
 * as an unsigned char cast to an int, or EOF when nothing is left
 * in the buffer
 */
int __wrap_getc(FILE *stream) {
    assert_true(stream == message_stream);
    return buffer_getc_index == buffer_getc_len
           ? EOF
           : buffer_getc[buffer_getc_index++];
}

/**
 * A mock putc function that put character to buffer
 * @param[in] c
 * @param[in] stream
 * @return the character written as an unsigned char cast to an int or EOF when buffer is full
 */
int __wrap_putc(int c, FILE *stream) {
    assert_true(stream == message_stream);
    if (buffer_putc_len == TEST_BUFFER_SIZE) {
        return EOF;
    }
    buffer_putc[buffer_putc_len++] = (uint8_t) c;
    return c;
}

/**
 * A mock fprintf function that checks the value of strings printed to the
 * standard error stream or output stream.
 */
int __wrap_fprintf(FILE *file, const char *format, ...) {
    int return_value;
    va_list args;
    assert_true(file == stderr);
    va_start(args, format);
    return_value = vsnprintf(buffer_stderr, sizeof(buffer_stderr),
                             format, args);
    va_end(args);
    return return_value;
}

/*
 * Wrap for exit(int) function
 **/
void __wrap_exit(int status) {
    (void)status;
    return;
}

/**
 * Create test stream with tmpfile()
 *
 * Run once before tests.
 * @param state unused (required by cmocka API)
 */
static int test_group_setup(void **state) {
    (void) state;
    message_stream = tmpfile();
    bzero(buffer_putc, TEST_BUFFER_SIZE);
    buffer_putc_len = 0u;
    uint8_t message[] = { // "write_message"
            0x80, // 10000000
    };
    write_message(message_stream, message, sizeof(message));
    if (buffer_putc_len != 3
        || buffer_putc[0] != 0x7E
        || buffer_putc[2] != 0x7E) {
        return 1;
    }
    if (buffer_putc[1] == 0x80) { // 10000000
        mode = MSB_FIRST;
        return 0;
    }
    if (buffer_putc[1] == 0x01) { // 00000001
        mode = LSB_FIRST;
        return 0;
    }
    return 1;
}

/**
 * Close test stream.
 * Run once after tests.
 * @param state unused (required by cmocka API)
 */
static int test_group_teardown(void **state) {
    (void) state;
    fclose(message_stream);
    return 0;
}

/**
 * Free buffers needed by tests.
 * Run before each test.
 * @param state unused (required by cmocka API)
 */
static int test_setup(void **state) {
    (void) state;
    bzero(buffer_stderr, TEST_BUFFER_SIZE);
    bzero(buffer_putc, TEST_BUFFER_SIZE);
    buffer_putc_len = 0u;
    bzero(buffer_getc, TEST_BUFFER_SIZE);
    buffer_getc_len = 0u;
    buffer_getc_index = 0u;
    return 0;
}

static void example_test_write_empty_message(void **state) {
    (void) state;
    const uint8_t message[1] = {0};
    ssize_t message_len = write_message(message_stream, message, 0);

    const uint8_t expected[] = {
            0x7E,
            0x7E,
    };
    // Check buffer
    assert_int_equal(message_len, 0);
    assert_int_equal(buffer_putc_len, 2);
    assert_memory_equal(buffer_putc, expected, 2);
    // Check error string
    assert_string_equal(buffer_stderr, "");
}

static void example_test_write_message(void **state) {
    (void) state;
    const uint8_t message[] = { // "write_message"
            0x77, // 01110111
            0x72, // 01110010
            0x69, // 01101001
            0x74, // 01110100
            0x65, // 01100101
            0x5F, // 01011111
            0x74, // 01110100
            0x65, // 01100101
            0x73, // 01110011
            0x74, // 01110100
    };
    ssize_t message_len = write_message(message_stream, message, sizeof(message));
    const uint8_t expected_msb[] = {
            0x7E, // 01111110
            0x77, // 01110111
            0x72, // 01110010
            0x69, // 01101001
            0x74, // 01110100
            0x65, // 01100101
            0x5F, // 01011111
            0x3A, // 00111010
            0x32, // 00110010
            0xB9, // 10111001
            0xBA, // 10111010
            0x3F, // 00111111
            0x7F, // 01111111
    };
    const uint8_t expected_lsb[] = {
            0x7E, // 01111110
            0xEE, // 11101110
            0x4E, // 01001110
            0x96, // 10010110
            0x2E, // 00101110
            0xA6, // 10100110
            0xFA, // 11111010
            0x5C, // 01011100
            0x4C, // 01001100
            0x9D, // 10011101
            0x5D, // 01011101
            0xFC, // 11111100
            0xFE, // 11111110
    };
    // Check buffer
    assert_int_equal(message_len, sizeof(message));
    assert_int_equal(buffer_putc_len, 13);
    if (mode == MSB_FIRST) {
        assert_memory_equal(buffer_putc, expected_msb, buffer_putc_len);
    } else {
        assert_memory_equal(buffer_putc, expected_lsb, buffer_putc_len);
    }
    // Check error string
    assert_string_equal(buffer_stderr, "");
}

static void example_test_read_empty_message(void **state) {
    (void) state;
    uint8_t message[MAX_MESSAGE_LEN] = {0};
    buffer_getc[0] = 0x7E;
    buffer_getc[1] = 0x7E;
    buffer_getc_len = 2;
    ssize_t message_len = read_message(message_stream, message);
    assert_int_equal(message_len, 0);
    assert_string_equal(buffer_stderr, "");
}

static void example_test_read_message(void **state) {
    (void) state;
    uint8_t message[MAX_MESSAGE_LEN] = {0}; // "read_test"
    if (mode == MSB_FIRST) {
        buffer_getc[0] = 0x7E; // 01111110
        buffer_getc[1] = 0x72; // 01110010
        buffer_getc[2] = 0x65; // 01100101
        buffer_getc[3] = 0x61; // 01100001
        buffer_getc[4] = 0x64; // 01100100
        buffer_getc[5] = 0x5F; // 01011111
        buffer_getc[6] = 0x3A; // 00111010
        buffer_getc[7] = 0x32; // 00110010
        buffer_getc[8] = 0xB9; // 10111001
        buffer_getc[9] = 0xBA; // 10111010
        buffer_getc[10] = 0x3F; // 00111111
        buffer_getc[11] = 0x7F; // 01111111
    } else {
        buffer_getc[0] = 0x7E; // 01111110
        buffer_getc[1] = 0x4E; // 01001110
        buffer_getc[2] = 0xA6; // 10100110
        buffer_getc[3] = 0x86; // 10000110
        buffer_getc[4] = 0x26; // 00100110
        buffer_getc[5] = 0xFA; // 11111010
        buffer_getc[6] = 0x5C; // 01011100
        buffer_getc[7] = 0x4C; // 01001100
        buffer_getc[8] = 0x9D; // 10011101
        buffer_getc[9] = 0x5D; // 01011101
        buffer_getc[10] = 0xFC; // 11111100
        buffer_getc[11] = 0xFE; // 11111110
    }
    buffer_getc_len = 12;
    ssize_t message_len = read_message(message_stream, message);
    const uint8_t expected[] = { // "read_test"
            0x72, // 01110010
            0x65, // 01100101
            0x61, // 01100001
            0x64, // 01100100
            0x5F, // 01011111
            0x74, // 01110100
            0x65, // 01100101
            0x73, // 01110011
            0x74, // 01110100
    };
    assert_int_equal(message_len, 9);
    assert_memory_equal(message, expected, message_len);
    assert_string_equal(buffer_stderr, "");
}

static void example_test_read_with_prefix_bits_1(void **state) {
    (void) state;
    uint8_t message[MAX_MESSAGE_LEN] = {0}; // "read_test"
    if (mode == MSB_FIRST) {
        buffer_getc[0] = 0xBF; // 10111111
        buffer_getc[1] = 0x39; // 00111001
        buffer_getc[2] = 0x32; // 00110010
        buffer_getc[3] = 0xB0; // 10110000
        buffer_getc[4] = 0xB2; // 10110010
        buffer_getc[5] = 0x2F; // 00101111
        buffer_getc[6] = 0x9D; // 10011101
        buffer_getc[7] = 0x19; // 00011001
        buffer_getc[8] = 0x5C; // 01011100
        buffer_getc[9] = 0xDD; // 11011101
        buffer_getc[10] = 0x1F; // 00011111
        buffer_getc[11] = 0xBF; // 10111111
    } else {
        buffer_getc[0] = 0xFD; // 11111101
        buffer_getc[1] = 0x9C; // 10011100
        buffer_getc[2] = 0x4C; // 01001100
        buffer_getc[3] = 0x0D; // 00001101
        buffer_getc[4] = 0x4D; // 01001101
        buffer_getc[5] = 0xF4; // 11110100
        buffer_getc[6] = 0xB9; // 10111001
        buffer_getc[7] = 0x98; // 10011000
        buffer_getc[8] = 0x3A; // 00111010
        buffer_getc[9] = 0xBB; // 10111011
        buffer_getc[10] = 0xF8; // 11111000
        buffer_getc[11] = 0xFD; // 11111101
    }
    buffer_getc_len = 12;
    ssize_t message_len = read_message(message_stream, message);
    const uint8_t expected[] = { // "read_test"
            0x72, // 01110010
            0x65, // 01100101
            0x61, // 01100001
            0x64, // 01100100
            0x5F, // 01011111
            0x74, // 01110100
            0x65, // 01100101
            0x73, // 01110011
            0x74, // 01110100
    };
    assert_int_equal(message_len, 9);
    assert_memory_equal(message, expected, message_len);
    assert_string_equal(buffer_stderr, "");
}

static void example_test_write_read_empty_message(void **state) {
    (void) state;
    const char *message_written = "";
    size_t len = strlen(message_written);
    write_message(message_stream, message_written, len);
    memcpy(buffer_getc, buffer_putc, buffer_putc_len);
    buffer_getc_len = buffer_putc_len;
    char message_read[MAX_MESSAGE_LEN] = {0};
    read_message(message_stream, message_read);

    assert_int_equal(strlen(message_read), len);
    assert_string_equal(message_read, message_written);
    assert_string_equal(buffer_stderr, "");
}

static void example_test_write_read_message(void **state) {
    (void) state;
    const char *message_written = "write_read_test";
    size_t len = strlen(message_written);
    ssize_t message_written_len = write_message(message_stream, message_written, len);
    memcpy(buffer_getc, buffer_putc, buffer_putc_len);
    buffer_getc_len = buffer_putc_len;
    char message_read[MAX_MESSAGE_LEN] = {0};
    ssize_t message_read_len = read_message(message_stream, message_read);

    assert_int_equal(message_written_len, len);
    assert_int_equal(message_read_len, len);
    assert_int_equal(strlen(message_read), len);
    assert_string_equal(message_read, message_written);
    assert_string_equal(buffer_stderr, "");
}

int main() {
    const struct CMUnitTest tests[] = {
            cmocka_unit_test_setup(example_test_write_empty_message, test_setup),
            cmocka_unit_test_setup(example_test_write_message, test_setup),
            cmocka_unit_test_setup(example_test_read_empty_message, test_setup),
            cmocka_unit_test_setup(example_test_read_message, test_setup),
            cmocka_unit_test_setup(example_test_read_with_prefix_bits_1, test_setup),
            cmocka_unit_test_setup(example_test_write_read_empty_message, test_setup),
            cmocka_unit_test_setup(example_test_write_read_message, test_setup),
    };

    return cmocka_run_group_tests(tests, test_group_setup, test_group_teardown);
}
#include "protocol.h"

#include <stdarg.h>
#include <stddef.h>
#include <setjmp.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <memory.h>
#include <inttypes.h>
#include <sys/types.h>

#include <cmocka.h>

#if defined(getc) || defined(putc) || defined(fprintf)
#error "Not handled yet: redefinition of stdio functions"
#endif

#define TEST_BUFFER_SIZE 512
static char buffer_stderr[TEST_BUFFER_SIZE];
static volatile size_t buffer_putc_len;
static uint8_t buffer_putc[TEST_BUFFER_SIZE];
static size_t buffer_getc_len;
static size_t buffer_getc_index;
static uint8_t buffer_getc[TEST_BUFFER_SIZE];

static FILE *message_stream;

static enum {
    UNDEFINED,
    MSB_FIRST,
    LSB_FIRST,
} mode = UNDEFINED;

/**
 * A mock getc function that get character from buffer
 * @param[in] stream
 * @return reads the next character from buffer and returns it
 * as an unsigned char cast to an int, or EOF when nothing is left
 * in the buffer
 */
int __wrap_getc(FILE *stream) {
    assert_true(stream == message_stream);
    return buffer_getc_index == buffer_getc_len
           ? EOF
           : buffer_getc[buffer_getc_index++];
}

/**
 * A mock putc function that put character to buffer
 * @param[in] c
 * @param[in] stream
 * @return the character written as an unsigned char cast to an int or EOF when buffer is full
 */
int __wrap_putc(int c, FILE *stream) {
    assert_true(stream == message_stream);
    if (buffer_putc_len == TEST_BUFFER_SIZE) {
        return EOF;
    }
    buffer_putc[buffer_putc_len++] = (uint8_t) c;
    return c;
}

/**
 * A mock fprintf function that checks the value of strings printed to the
 * standard error stream or output stream.
 */
int __wrap_fprintf(FILE *file, const char *format, ...) {
    int return_value;
    va_list args;
    assert_true(file == stderr);
    va_start(args, format);
    return_value = vsnprintf(buffer_stderr, sizeof(buffer_stderr),
                             format, args);
    va_end(args);
    return return_value;
}

/*
 * Wrap for exit(int) function
 **/
void __wrap_exit(int status) {
    (void)status;
    return;
}

/**
 * Create test stream with tmpfile()
 *
 * Run once before tests.
 * @param state unused (required by cmocka API)
 */
static int test_group_setup(void **state) {
    (void) state;
    message_stream = tmpfile();
    bzero(buffer_putc, TEST_BUFFER_SIZE);
    buffer_putc_len = 0u;
    uint8_t message[] = { // "write_message"
            0x80, // 10000000
    };
    write_message(message_stream, message, sizeof(message));
    if (buffer_putc_len != 3
        || buffer_putc[0] != 0x7E
        || buffer_putc[2] != 0x7E) {
        return 1;
    }
    if (buffer_putc[1] == 0x80) { // 10000000
        mode = MSB_FIRST;
        return 0;
    }
    if (buffer_putc[1] == 0x01) { // 00000001
        mode = LSB_FIRST;
        return 0;
    }
    return 1;
}

/**
 * Close test stream.
 * Run once after tests.
 * @param state unused (required by cmocka API)
 */
static int test_group_teardown(void **state) {
    (void) state;
    fclose(message_stream);
    return 0;
}

/**
 * Free buffers needed by tests.
 * Run before each test.
 * @param state unused (required by cmocka API)
 */
static int test_setup(void **state) {
    (void) state;
    bzero(buffer_stderr, TEST_BUFFER_SIZE);
    bzero(buffer_putc, TEST_BUFFER_SIZE);
    buffer_putc_len = 0u;
    bzero(buffer_getc, TEST_BUFFER_SIZE);
    buffer_getc_len = 0u;
    buffer_getc_index = 0u;
    return 0;
}

            0x7E,
            0x7E,
    };

    assert_int_equal(buffer_putc_len, 2);
    assert_memory_equal(buffer_putc, expected, 2);
    // Check error string

}

static void example_test_write_message(void **state) {
    (void) state;
    const uint8_t message[] = { // "write_message"
            0x77, // 01110111
            0x72, // 01110010
            0x69, // 01101001
            0x74, // 01110100
            0x65, // 01100101
            0x5F, // 01011111
            0x74, // 01110100
            0x65, // 01100101
            0x73, // 01110011
            0x74, // 01110100
    };
    ssize_t message_len = write_message(message_stream, message, sizeof(message));
    const uint8_t expected_msb[] = {
            0x7E, // 01111110
            0x77, // 01110111
            0x72, // 01110010
            0x69, // 01101001
            0x74, // 01110100
            0x65, // 01100101
            0x5F, // 01011111
            0x3A, // 00111010
            0x32, // 00110010
            0xB9, // 10111001
            0xBA, // 10111010
            0x3F, // 00111111
            0x7F, // 01111111
    };
    const uint8_t expected_lsb[] = {
            0x7E, // 01111110
            0xEE, // 11101110
            0x4E, // 01001110
            0x96, // 10010110
            0x2E, // 00101110
            0xA6, // 10100110
            0xFA, // 11111010
            0x5C, // 01011100
            0x4C, // 01001100
            0x9D, // 10011101
            0x5D, // 01011101
            0xFC, // 11111100
            0xFE, // 11111110
    };
    // Check buffer

    assert_int_equal(buffer_putc_len, 13);
    if (mode == MSB_FIRST) {
        assert_memory_equal(buffer_putc, expected_msb, buffer_putc_len);
    } else {
        assert_memory_equal(buffer_putc, expected_lsb, buffer_putc_len);
    }
    // Check error string
    assert_string_equal(buffer_stderr, "");
}

#include "bmp.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>

#pragma pack(push, 1)
typedef struct {
  uint16_t type;
  uint32_t size;
  uint32_t reserved;
  uint32_t offset;
} bmp_header_t;

typedef struct {
  uint32_t size;
  int32_t width;
  int32_t height;
  uint16_t planes;
  uint16_t bit_count;
  uint32_t compression;
  uint32_t image_size;
  uint32_t x_ppm;
  uint32_t y_ppm;
  uint32_t colors_used;
  uint32_t colors_important;
} bmp_info_t;
#pragma pack(pop)

static uint32_t calc_row_size(uint32_t width, uint16_t bit_count) {
  uint32_t bits = width * bit_count;
  return ((bits + 31) / 32) * 4;
}

void bmp_free(bmp_image_t *image) {
  if (!image)
    return;
  if (image->data)
    free(image->data);
  free(image);
}

bool bmp_is_valid(const bmp_image_t *image) {
  if (!image)
    return false;
  if (image->bit_count != 8 && image->bit_count != 24)
    return false;
  if (image->width <= 0 || image->height == 0)
    return false;
  if (!image->data)
    return false;
  return true;
}

bmp_image_t *bmp_read(const char *filename) {
  FILE *file = fopen(filename, "rb");
  if (!file) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot open file '%s'\n", filename);
    return NULL;
  }

  bmp_header_t header;
  bmp_info_t info;

  if (fread(&header, sizeof(header), 1, file) != 1 ||
      fread(&info, sizeof(info), 1, file) != 1) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot read BMP headers from '%s'\n", filename);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (header.type != 0x4D42) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: File '%s' is not a BMP file (wrong signature)\n",
            filename);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (info.size != 40) {
    fprintf(
        stderr,
        "Error: Unsupported BMP header size in '%s' (%u bytes, expected 40)\n",
        filename, info.size);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (info.compression != 0) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Compression is not supported in '%s'\n", filename);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (info.planes != 1) {
    fprintf(stderr,
            "Error: Invalid number of planes in '%s' (%u, expected 1)\n",
            filename, info.planes);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (info.bit_count != 8 && info.bit_count != 24) {
    fprintf(stderr,
            "Error: Unsupported bit depth in '%s' (%u bits, only 8 and 24 "
            "supported)\n",
            filename, info.bit_count);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (info.width == 0 || info.height == 0) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Invalid image dimensions in '%s' (%dx%d)\n",
            filename, info.width, info.height);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  fseek(file, 0, SEEK_END);
  long file_size = ftell(file);

  if (header.size > (uint32_t)file_size) {
    fprintf(stderr,
            "Error: BMP header in '%s' claims file size %u bytes, but actual "
            "size is %ld bytes\n",
            filename, header.size, file_size);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  fseek(file, sizeof(header) + sizeof(info), SEEK_SET);

  bmp_image_t *image = malloc(sizeof(bmp_image_t));
  if (!image) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Memory allocation failed for image structure\n");
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  image->width = info.width;
  image->height = info.height;
  image->bit_count = info.bit_count;
  image->row_size = calc_row_size((uint32_t)image->width, image->bit_count);

  if (image->bit_count == 8) {
    if (fread(image->palette, 4, 256, file) != 256) {
      fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot read palette from '%s'\n", filename);
      fclose(file);
      free(image);
      return NULL;
    }
  }

  uint32_t expected_data_size = image->row_size * image->height;

  if (header.offset + expected_data_size > header.size) {
    fprintf(stderr,
            "Error: Image data in '%s' exceeds size claimed in BMP header\n",
            filename);
    fprintf(stderr, "  Offset: %u, Expected data size: %u, Header size: %u\n",
            header.offset, expected_data_size, header.size);
    fclose(file);
    free(image);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (header.offset + expected_data_size > (uint32_t)file_size) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Image data in '%s' exceeds file size\n", filename);
    fprintf(stderr, "  Offset: %u, Expected data size: %u, File size: %ld\n",
            header.offset, expected_data_size, file_size);
    fclose(file);
    free(image);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (header.offset > header.size ||
      header.offset < sizeof(header) + sizeof(info)) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Invalid data offset in '%s' (%u)\n", filename,
            header.offset);
    fclose(file);
    free(image);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (fseek(file, header.offset, SEEK_SET) != 0) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot seek to pixel data in '%s' at offset %u\n",
            filename, header.offset);
    fclose(file);
    free(image);
    return NULL;
  }

  image->data = malloc(expected_data_size);
  if (!image->data) {
    fprintf(stderr,
            "Error: Cannot allocate memory for pixel data in '%s' (%u bytes)\n",
            filename, expected_data_size);
    fclose(file);
    free(image);
    return NULL;
  }

  size_t bytes_read = fread(image->data, 1, expected_data_size, file);
  if (bytes_read != expected_data_size) {
    fprintf(stderr,
            "Error: Cannot read pixel data from '%s' (read %zu of %u bytes)\n",
            filename, bytes_read, expected_data_size);
    fclose(file);
    free(image->data);
    free(image);
    return NULL;
  }

  fclose(file);
  return image;
}

bool bmp_write(const bmp_image_t *image, const char *filename) {
  if (!bmp_is_valid(image)) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Invalid image\n");
    return false;
  }

  FILE *file = fopen(filename, "wb");
  if (!file) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot create file '%s'\n", filename);
    return false;
  }

  bmp_header_t header;
  bmp_info_t info;

  uint32_t palette_size = (image->bit_count == 8) ? 1024 : 0;
  uint32_t data_size = image->row_size * image->height;

  header.type = 0x4D42;
  header.size = sizeof(header) + sizeof(info) + palette_size + data_size;
  header.reserved = 0;
  header.offset = sizeof(header) + sizeof(info) + palette_size;

  info.size = 40;
  info.width = image->width;
  info.height = image->height;
  info.planes = 1;
  info.bit_count = image->bit_count;
  info.compression = 0;
  info.image_size = data_size;
  info.x_ppm = 0;
  info.y_ppm = 0;
  info.colors_used = (image->bit_count == 8) ? 256 : 0;
  info.colors_important = 0;

  fwrite(&header, sizeof(header), 1, file);
  fwrite(&info, sizeof(info), 1, file);

  if (image->bit_count == 8) {
    fwrite(image->palette, 4, 256, file);
  }

  fwrite(image->data, 1, data_size, file);

  fclose(file);
  return true;
}
#ifndef BMP_H
#define BMP_H

#include <stdbool.h>
#include <stdint.h>

typedef struct {
  int32_t width;
  int32_t height;
  uint16_t bit_count;
  uint32_t row_size;

  uint8_t *data;
  uint8_t palette[256][4];
} bmp_image_t;

bmp_image_t *bmp_read(const char *filename);
bool bmp_write(const bmp_image_t *image, const char *filename);
void bmp_free(bmp_image_t *image);

bool bmp_is_valid(const bmp_image_t *image);

#endif
#include "../bmp/bmp.h"
#include <stdio.h>

int main(int argc, char *argv[]) {
  if (argc != 3) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Expected 2 arguments\n");
    return 1;
  }

  bmp_image_t *img1 = bmp_read(argv[1]);
  bmp_image_t *img2 = bmp_read(argv[2]);

  if (!img1 || !img2) {
    if (img1)
      bmp_free(img1);
    if (img2)
      bmp_free(img2);
    return 1;
  }

  if (img1->bit_count != img2->bit_count) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Different bit depths\n");
    bmp_free(img1);
    bmp_free(img2);
    return 1;
  }

  if (img1->width != img2->width || img1->height != img2->height) {
    int32_t abs_height1 = (img1->height < 0) ? -img1->height : img1->height;
    int32_t abs_height2 = (img2->height < 0) ? -img2->height : img2->height;
    int32_t abs_width1 = (img1->width < 0) ? -img1->width : img1->width;
    int32_t abs_width2 = (img2->width < 0) ? -img2->width : img2->width;

    if (abs_width1 != abs_width2 || abs_height1 != abs_height2) {
      fprintf(stderr, "Error: Different dimensions\n");
      bmp_free(img1);
      bmp_free(img2);
      return 1;
    }
  }

  int diff_count = 0;
  int max_diffs = 100;
  bool first_diff = true;

  int32_t abs_height1 = (img1->height < 0) ? -img1->height : img1->height;
  int32_t abs_width1 = (img1->width < 0) ? -img1->width : img1->width;

  for (int32_t y = 0; y < abs_height1; y++) {
    int32_t row_idx1 = (img1->height < 0) ? y : (abs_height1 - 1 - y);
    int32_t row_idx2 = (img2->height < 0) ? y : (abs_height1 - 1 - y);

    uint8_t *row1 = img1->data + row_idx1 * img1->row_size;
    uint8_t *row2 = img2->data + row_idx2 * img2->row_size;

    for (int32_t x = 0; x < abs_width1; x++) {
      bool equal = false;

      if (img1->bit_count == 8) {
        uint8_t idx1 = row1[x];
        uint8_t idx2 = row2[x];

        equal = (img1->palette[idx1][0] == img2->palette[idx2][0] &&
                 img1->palette[idx1][1] == img2->palette[idx2][1] &&
                 img1->palette[idx1][2] == img2->palette[idx2][2]);
      } else { // 24-bit
        uint8_t *px1 = row1 + x * 3;
        uint8_t *px2 = row2 + x * 3;

        equal = (px1[0] == px2[0] && // Blue
                 px1[1] == px2[1] && // Green
                 px1[2] == px2[2]);  // Red
      }

      if (!equal) {
        if (first_diff) {
          fprintf(stderr, "Next pixels are different:\n");
          first_diff = false;
        }
        fprintf(stderr, "x%-6d y%-6d\n", x, y);
        diff_count++;

        if (diff_count >= max_diffs) {
          y = img1->height;
          break;
        }
      }
    }
  }

  bmp_free(img1);
  bmp_free(img2);

  if (diff_count == 0) {
    printf("Images are same\n");
    return 0;
  } else {
    return 2;
  }
}
#include "../bmp/bmp.h"
#include <stdio.h>

int main(int argc, char *argv[]) {
  if (argc != 3) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Expected 2 arguments\n");
    return 1;
  }

  bmp_image_t *image = bmp_read(argv[1]);
  if (!image) {
    return 1;
  }

  if (image->bit_count == 8) {
    for (int i = 0; i < 256; i++) {
      image->palette[i][0] = 255 - image->palette[i][0]; // Blue
      image->palette[i][1] = 255 - image->palette[i][1]; // Green
      image->palette[i][2] = 255 - image->palette[i][2]; // Red
    }
  } else if (image->bit_count == 24) {
    for (int32_t y = 0; y < image->height; y++) {
      uint8_t *row = image->data + y * image->row_size;
      for (int32_t x = 0; x < image->width; x++) {
        uint8_t *pixel = row + x * 3;
        pixel[0] = 255 - pixel[0]; // Blue
        pixel[1] = 255 - pixel[1]; // Green
        pixel[2] = 255 - pixel[2]; // Red
      }
    }
  }

  if (!bmp_write(image, argv[2])) {
    bmp_free(image);
    return 1;
  }

  bmp_free(image);
  return 0;
}
#include "bmp.h"
#include <errno.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>

#define BMP_TYPE 0x4D42

BMPImage *bmp_read(const char *filename) {
  FILE *file = fopen(filename, "rb");
  if (!file) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot open file '%s': %s\n", filename,
            strerror(errno));
    return NULL;
  }

  BMPImage *image = malloc(sizeof(BMPImage));
  if (!image) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Memory allocation failed\n");
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (fread(&image->file_header, sizeof(BMPFileHeader), 1, file) != 1) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot read BMP file header\n");
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (image->file_header.type != BMP_TYPE) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Not a valid BMP file (wrong signature)\n");
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (fread(&image->info_header, sizeof(BMPInfoHeader), 1, file) != 1) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot read BMP info header\n");
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (image->info_header.size != 40) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Unsupported BMP format (header size must be 40)\n");
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (image->info_header.bits_per_pixel != 8 &&
      image->info_header.bits_per_pixel != 24) {
    fprintf(stderr,
            "Error: Unsupported bit depth (%d). Only 8-bit and 24-bit are "
            "supported\n",
            image->info_header.bits_per_pixel);
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (image->info_header.width <= 0 || image->info_header.height == 0) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Invalid image dimensions (width=%d, height=%d)\n",
            image->info_header.width, image->info_header.height);
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (image->info_header.compression != 0) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Compression is not supported\n");
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  image->color_table = NULL;
  if (image->info_header.bits_per_pixel == 8) {
    uint32_t color_table_size = image->info_header.colors_used;
    if (color_table_size == 0) {
      color_table_size = 256;
    }

    image->color_table = malloc(color_table_size * sizeof(RGBQuad));
    if (!image->color_table) {
      fprintf(stderr, "Error: Memory allocation for color table failed\n");
      free(image);
      fclose(file);
      return NULL;
    }

    size_t read_count =
        fread(image->color_table, sizeof(RGBQuad), color_table_size, file);
    if (read_count != color_table_size) {
      fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot read color table (expected %u, got %zu)\n",
              color_table_size, read_count);
      free(image->color_table);
      free(image);
      fclose(file);
      return NULL;
    }
  } else {
    fseek(file, image->file_header.offset, SEEK_SET);
  }

  image->row_size = bmp_calculate_row_size((uint32_t)image->info_header.width,
                                           image->info_header.bits_per_pixel);

  uint32_t height = (uint32_t)abs(image->info_header.height);
  image->actual_image_size = image->row_size * height;

  uint32_t required_size = image->file_header.offset + image->actual_image_size;
  if (required_size > image->file_header.size) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Image data exceeds size claimed in BMP header\n");
    fprintf(stderr, "  Offset: %u, Image data size: %u, Header file size: %u\n",
            image->file_header.offset, image->actual_image_size,
            image->file_header.size);
    if (image->color_table)
      free(image->color_table);
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (image->info_header.image_size != 0) {
    if (image->info_header.image_size > image->actual_image_size) {
      uint32_t required_with_header_size =
          image->file_header.offset + image->info_header.image_size;
      if (required_with_header_size > image->file_header.size) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: Image size in header exceeds file size\n");
        if (image->color_table)
          free(image->color_table);
        free(image);
        fclose(file);
        return NULL;
      }
    }
  }

  image->pixel_data = malloc(image->actual_image_size);
  if (!image->pixel_data) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Memory allocation for pixel data failed\n");
    if (image->color_table)
      free(image->color_table);
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  size_t read_size =
      fread(image->pixel_data, 1, image->actual_image_size, file);
  if (read_size != image->actual_image_size) {
    fprintf(stderr,
            "Error: Cannot read pixel data (expected %u bytes, got %zu)\n",
            image->actual_image_size, read_size);
    free(image->pixel_data);
    if (image->color_table)
      free(image->color_table);
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  fclose(file);
  return image;
}

bool bmp_write(BMPImage *image, const char *filename) {
  if (!bmp_is_valid(image)) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Invalid BMP image structure\n");
    return false;
  }

  FILE *file = fopen(filename, "wb");
  if (!file) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot create file '%s': %s\n", filename,
            strerror(errno));
    return false;
  }

  if (fwrite(&image->file_header, sizeof(BMPFileHeader), 1, file) != 1) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot write BMP file header\n");
    fclose(file);
    return false;
  }

  if (fwrite(&image->info_header, sizeof(BMPInfoHeader), 1, file) != 1) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot write BMP info header\n");
    fclose(file);
    return false;
  }

  if (image->info_header.bits_per_pixel == 8 && image->color_table) {
    uint32_t color_table_size = image->info_header.colors_used;
    if (color_table_size == 0) {
      color_table_size = 256;
    }

    size_t written =
        fwrite(image->color_table, sizeof(RGBQuad), color_table_size, file);
    if (written != color_table_size) {
      fprintf(stderr,
              "Error: Cannot write color table (expected %u, wrote %zu)\n",
              color_table_size, written);
      fclose(file);
      return false;
    }
  }

  size_t written = fwrite(image->pixel_data, 1, image->actual_image_size, file);
  if (written != image->actual_image_size) {
    fprintf(stderr,
            "Error: Cannot write pixel data (expected %u bytes, wrote %zu)\n",
            image->actual_image_size, written);
    fclose(file);
    return false;
  }

  long current_size = ftell(file);
  if (current_size < 0) {
    perror("ftell");
    fclose(file);
    return false;
  }

  if ((uint32_t)current_size < image->file_header.size) {
    uint32_t padding = image->file_header.size - (uint32_t)current_size;
    uint8_t zero = 0;
    for (uint32_t i = 0; i < padding; i++) {
      if (fwrite(&zero, 1, 1, file) != 1) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot write padding\n");
        fclose(file);
        return false;
      }
    }
  } else if ((uint32_t)current_size > image->file_header.size) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Written file larger than header claims\n");
    fclose(file);
    return false;
  }

  fclose(file);
  return true;
}

void bmp_free(BMPImage *image) {
  if (image) {
    if (image->color_table) {
      free(image->color_table);
    }
    if (image->pixel_data) {
      free(image->pixel_data);
    }
    free(image);
  }
}

bool bmp_is_valid(BMPImage *image) {
  if (!image)
    return false;
  if (image->file_header.type != BMP_TYPE)
    return false;
  if (image->info_header.size != 40)
    return false;
  if (image->info_header.bits_per_pixel != 8 &&
      image->info_header.bits_per_pixel != 24)
    return false;
  if (image->info_header.width <= 0)
    return false;
  if (image->info_header.height == 0)
    return false;
  if (image->info_header.compression != 0)
    return false;
  if (!image->pixel_data)
    return false;
  if (image->info_header.bits_per_pixel == 8 && !image->color_table)
    return false;

  uint32_t calculated_row_size = bmp_calculate_row_size(
      (uint32_t)image->info_header.width, image->info_header.bits_per_pixel);
  if (image->row_size != calculated_row_size)
    return false;

  uint32_t height = (uint32_t)abs(image->info_header.height);
  uint32_t calculated_image_size = image->row_size * height;
  if (image->actual_image_size != calculated_image_size)
    return false;

  if (image->info_header.image_size != 0 &&
      image->info_header.image_size != calculated_image_size) {
    if (image->info_header.image_size > calculated_image_size) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  return true;
}

uint8_t *bmp_get_pixel_address(BMPImage *image, int32_t x, int32_t y) {
  if (!image || !image->pixel_data)
    return NULL;
  if (x < 0 || x >= image->info_header.width)
    return NULL;

  int32_t height_abs = abs(image->info_header.height);
  if (y < 0 || y >= height_abs)
    return NULL;

  uint32_t memory_row;
  if (image->info_header.height > 0) {
    memory_row = (uint32_t)y;
  } else {
    memory_row = (uint32_t)(height_abs - 1 - y);
  }

  uint32_t pixel_size = image->info_header.bits_per_pixel / 8;
  if (pixel_size == 0)
    pixel_size = 1;

  uint32_t offset = memory_row * image->row_size + (uint32_t)x * pixel_size;

  if (offset >= image->actual_image_size)
    return NULL;

  return image->pixel_data + offset;
}

bool bmp_is_same_format(BMPImage *img1, BMPImage *img2) {
  if (!img1 || !img2)
    return false;

  return (img1->info_header.bits_per_pixel == img2->info_header.bits_per_pixel);
}

uint32_t bmp_calculate_row_size(uint32_t width, uint16_t bpp) {
  uint32_t row_size = (width * bpp + 7) / 8;
  return (row_size + 3) & ~3;
}
#include "bmp.h"
#include <errno.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>

#define BMP_TYPE 0x4D42

BMPImage *bmp_read(const char *filename) {
  FILE *file = fopen(filename, "rb");
  if (!file) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot open file '%s': %s\n", filename,
            strerror(errno));
    return NULL;
  }

  BMPImage *image = malloc(sizeof(BMPImage));
  if (!image) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Memory allocation failed\n");
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (fread(&image->file_header, sizeof(BMPFileHeader), 1, file) != 1) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot read BMP file header\n");
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (image->file_header.type != BMP_TYPE) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Not a valid BMP file (wrong signature)\n");
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (fread(&image->info_header, sizeof(BMPInfoHeader), 1, file) != 1) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot read BMP info header\n");
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (image->info_header.size != 40) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Unsupported BMP format (header size must be 40)\n");
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (image->info_header.bits_per_pixel != 8 &&
      image->info_header.bits_per_pixel != 24) {
    fprintf(stderr,
            "Error: Unsupported bit depth (%d). Only 8-bit and 24-bit are "
            "supported\n",
            image->info_header.bits_per_pixel);
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (image->info_header.width <= 0 || image->info_header.height == 0) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Invalid image dimensions (width=%d, height=%d)\n",
            image->info_header.width, image->info_header.height);
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (image->info_header.compression != 0) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Compression is not supported\n");
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  image->color_table = NULL;
  if (image->info_header.bits_per_pixel == 8) {
    uint32_t color_table_size = image->info_header.colors_used;
    if (color_table_size == 0) {
      color_table_size = 256;
    }

    image->color_table = malloc(color_table_size * sizeof(RGBQuad));
    if (!image->color_table) {
      fprintf(stderr, "Error: Memory allocation for color table failed\n");
      free(image);
      fclose(file);
      return NULL;
    }

    size_t read_count =
        fread(image->color_table, sizeof(RGBQuad), color_table_size, file);
    if (read_count != color_table_size) {
      fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot read color table (expected %u, got %zu)\n",
              color_table_size, read_count);
      free(image->color_table);
      free(image);
      fclose(file);
      return NULL;
    }
  } else {
    fseek(file, image->file_header.offset, SEEK_SET);
  }

  image->row_size = bmp_calculate_row_size((uint32_t)image->info_header.width,
                                           image->info_header.bits_per_pixel);

  uint32_t height = (uint32_t)abs(image->info_header.height);
  image->actual_image_size = image->row_size * height;

  uint32_t required_size = image->file_header.offset + image->actual_image_size;
  if (required_size > image->file_header.size) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Image data exceeds size claimed in BMP header\n");
    fprintf(stderr, "  Offset: %u, Image data size: %u, Header file size: %u\n",
            image->file_header.offset, image->actual_image_size,
            image->file_header.size);
    if (image->color_table)
      free(image->color_table);
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  if (image->info_header.image_size != 0) {
    if (image->info_header.image_size > image->actual_image_size) {
      uint32_t required_with_header_size =
          image->file_header.offset + image->info_header.image_size;
      if (required_with_header_size > image->file_header.size) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: Image size in header exceeds file size\n");
        if (image->color_table)
          free(image->color_table);
        free(image);
        fclose(file);
        return NULL;
      }
    }
  }

  image->pixel_data = malloc(image->actual_image_size);
  if (!image->pixel_data) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Memory allocation for pixel data failed\n");
    if (image->color_table)
      free(image->color_table);
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  size_t read_size =
      fread(image->pixel_data, 1, image->actual_image_size, file);
  if (read_size != image->actual_image_size) {
    fprintf(stderr,
            "Error: Cannot read pixel data (expected %u bytes, got %zu)\n",
            image->actual_image_size, read_size);
    free(image->pixel_data);
    if (image->color_table)
      free(image->color_table);
    free(image);
    fclose(file);
    return NULL;
  }

  fclose(file);
  return image;
}

bool bmp_write(BMPImage *image, const char *filename) {
  if (!bmp_is_valid(image)) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Invalid BMP image structure\n");
    return false;
  }

  FILE *file = fopen(filename, "wb");
  if (!file) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot create file '%s': %s\n", filename,
            strerror(errno));
    return false;
  }

  if (fwrite(&image->file_header, sizeof(BMPFileHeader), 1, file) != 1) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot write BMP file header\n");
    fclose(file);
    return false;
  }

  if (fwrite(&image->info_header, sizeof(BMPInfoHeader), 1, file) != 1) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot write BMP info header\n");
    fclose(file);
    return false;
  }

  if (image->info_header.bits_per_pixel == 8 && image->color_table) {
    uint32_t color_table_size = image->info_header.colors_used;
    if (color_table_size == 0) {
      color_table_size = 256;
    }

    size_t written =
        fwrite(image->color_table, sizeof(RGBQuad), color_table_size, file);
    if (written != color_table_size) {
      fprintf(stderr,
              "Error: Cannot write color table (expected %u, wrote %zu)\n",
              color_table_size, written);
      fclose(file);
      return false;
    }
  }

  size_t written = fwrite(image->pixel_data, 1, image->actual_image_size, file);
  if (written != image->actual_image_size) {
    fprintf(stderr,
            "Error: Cannot write pixel data (expected %u bytes, wrote %zu)\n",
            image->actual_image_size, written);
    fclose(file);
    return false;
  }

  long current_size = ftell(file);
  if (current_size < 0) {
    perror("ftell");
    fclose(file);
    return false;
  }

  if ((uint32_t)current_size < image->file_header.size) {
    uint32_t padding = image->file_header.size - (uint32_t)current_size;
    uint8_t zero = 0;
    for (uint32_t i = 0; i < padding; i++) {
      if (fwrite(&zero, 1, 1, file) != 1) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Error: Cannot write padding\n");
        fclose(file);
        return false;
      }
    }
  } else if ((uint32_t)current_size > image->file_header.size) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Error: Written file larger than header claims\n");
    fclose(file);
    return false;
  }

  fclose(file);
  return true;
}

void bmp_free(BMPImage *image) {
  if (image) {
    if (image->color_table) {
      free(image->color_table);
    }
    if (image->pixel_data) {
      free(image->pixel_data);
    }
    free(image);
  }
}

bool bmp_is_valid(BMPImage *image) {
  if (!image)
    return false;
  if (image->file_header.type != BMP_TYPE)
    return false;
  if (image->info_header.size != 40)
    return false;
  if (image->info_header.bits_per_pixel != 8 &&
      image->info_header.bits_per_pixel != 24)
    return false;
  if (image->info_header.width <= 0)
    return false;
  if (image->info_header.height == 0)
    return false;
  if (image->info_header.compression != 0)
    return false;
  if (!image->pixel_data)
    return false;
  if (image->info_header.bits_per_pixel == 8 && !image->color_table)
    return false;

  uint32_t calculated_row_size = bmp_calculate_row_size(
      (uint32_t)image->info_header.width, image->info_header.bits_per_pixel);
  if (image->row_size != calculated_row_size)
    return false;

  uint32_t height = (uint32_t)abs(image->info_header.height);
  uint32_t calculated_image_size = image->row_size * height;
  if (image->actual_image_size != calculated_image_size)
    return false;

  if (image->info_header.image_size != 0 &&
      image->info_header.image_size != calculated_image_size) {
    if (image->info_header.image_size > calculated_image_size) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  return true;
}

uint8_t *bmp_get_pixel_address(BMPImage *image, int32_t x, int32_t y) {
  if (!image || !image->pixel_data)
    return NULL;
  if (x < 0 || x >= image->info_header.width)
    return NULL;

  int32_t height_abs = abs(image->info_header.height);
  if (y < 0 || y >= height_abs)
    return NULL;

  uint32_t memory_row;
  if (image->info_header.height > 0) {
    memory_row = (uint32_t)y;
  } else {
    memory_row = (uint32_t)(height_abs - 1 - y);
  }

  uint32_t pixel_size = image->info_header.bits_per_pixel / 8;
  if (pixel_size == 0)
    pixel_size = 1;

  uint32_t offset = memory_row * image->row_size + (uint32_t)x * pixel_size;

  if (offset >= image->actual_image_size)
    return NULL;

  return image->pixel_data + offset;
}

bool bmp_is_same_format(BMPImage *img1, BMPImage *img2) {
  if (!img1 || !img2)
    return false;

  return (img1->info_header.bits_per_pixel == img2->info_header.bits_per_pixel);
}

uint32_t bmp_calculate_row_size(uint32_t width, uint16_t bpp) {
  uint32_t row_size = (width * bpp + 7) / 8;
  return (row_size + 3) & ~3;
}
#ifndef BMP_H
#define BMP_H

#include <stdbool.h>
#include <stdint.h>

#pragma pack(push, 1)
typedef struct {
  uint16_t type; // "BM"
  uint32_t size; // File size in bytes
  uint16_t reserved1;
  uint16_t reserved2;
  uint32_t offset; // Offset to pixel data
} BMPFileHeader;

typedef struct {
  uint32_t size;              // Header size (must be 40)
  int32_t width;              // Image width in pixels
  int32_t height;             // Image height in pixels (positive = bottom-up)
  uint16_t planes;            // Number of color planes (must be 1)
  uint16_t bits_per_pixel;    // (8 or 24)
  uint32_t compression;       // Compression type (0 = none)
  uint32_t image_size;        // Image size in bytes (0 for uncompressed)
  int32_t x_pixels_per_meter; // Horizontal resolution
  int32_t y_pixels_per_meter; // Vertical resolution
  uint32_t colors_used;       // Number of colors in palette
  uint32_t colors_important;
} BMPInfoHeader;

typedef struct {
  uint8_t blue;
  uint8_t green;
  uint8_t red;
  uint8_t reserved; // Should be 0
} RGBQuad;
#pragma pack(pop)

typedef struct {
  BMPFileHeader file_header;
  BMPInfoHeader info_header;
  RGBQuad *color_table; // For 8-bit images
  uint8_t *pixel_data;
  uint32_t row_size;          // Size of one row in bytes (with padding)
  uint32_t actual_image_size; // Actual image data size
} BMPImage;

BMPImage *bmp_read(const char *filename);
bool bmp_write(BMPImage *image, const char *filename);
void bmp_free(BMPImage *image);
bool bmp_is_valid(BMPImage *image);
uint8_t *bmp_get_pixel_address(BMPImage *image, int32_t x, int32_t y);
bool bmp_is_same_format(BMPImage *img1, BMPImage *img2);
uint32_t bmp_calculate_row_size(uint32_t width, uint16_t bpp);

#endif
#ifndef BMP_H
#define BMP_H

#include <stdbool.h>
#include <stdint.h>

#pragma pack(push, 1)
typedef struct {
  uint16_t type; // "BM"
  uint32_t size; // File size in bytes
  uint16_t reserved1;
  uint16_t reserved2;
  uint32_t offset; // Offset to pixel data
} BMPFileHeader;

typedef struct {
  uint32_t size;              // Header size (must be 40)
  int32_t width;              // Image width in pixels
  int32_t height;             // Image height in pixels (positive = bottom-up)
  uint16_t planes;            // Number of color planes (must be 1)
  uint16_t bits_per_pixel;    // (8 or 24)
  uint32_t compression;       // Compression type (0 = none)
  uint32_t image_size;        // Image size in bytes (0 for uncompressed)
  int32_t x_pixels_per_meter; // Horizontal resolution
  int32_t y_pixels_per_meter; // Vertical resolution
  uint32_t colors_used;       // Number of colors in palette
  uint32_t colors_important;
} BMPInfoHeader;

typedef struct {
  uint8_t blue;
  uint8_t green;
  uint8_t red;
  uint8_t reserved; // Should be 0
} RGBQuad;
#pragma pack(pop)

typedef struct {
  BMPFileHeader file_header;
  BMPInfoHeader info_header;
  RGBQuad *color_table; // For 8-bit images
  uint8_t *pixel_data;
  uint32_t row_size;          // Size of one row in bytes (with padding)
  uint32_t actual_image_size; // Actual image data size
} BMPImage;

BMPImage *bmp_read(const char *filename);
bool bmp_write(BMPImage *image, const char *filename);
void bmp_free(BMPImage *image);
bool bmp_is_valid(BMPImage *image);
uint8_t *bmp_get_pixel_address(BMPImage *image, int32_t x, int32_t y);
bool bmp_is_same_format(BMPImage *img1, BMPImage *img2);
